### **1. Student Dashboard Module - `student_dashboard.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from study_recommendations import recommend_next_resources
from research_notebook import load_notes, USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE
from board_of_education import APPROVED

def student_dashboard(student_id, subjects):
    """
    Visual, interactive dashboard for students.
    """
    print(f"\n=== Welcome Student {student_id} ===")

    # --- Notes Completion ---
    usage_file = USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE.format(student_id=student_id)
    usage = {}
    if os.path.exists(usage_file):
        with open(usage_file, "r") as f:
            usage = json.load(f)
    notes = load_notes(student_id)
    total_notes = len(notes)
    read_notes = sum(1 for n in notes if usage.get(str(n['id']), False))
    unread_notes = total_notes - read_notes

    plt.figure(figsize=(6, 6))
    plt.bar(["Read Notes", "Unread Notes"], [read_notes, unread_notes], color=['green', 'red'])
    plt.title("Notes Completion")
    plt.ylabel("Number of Notes")
    plt.show()

    print(f"Notes Read: {read_notes}/{total_notes}\n")

    # --- Grades Overview ---
    grades = {}
    for file in os.listdir(APPROVED) if os.path.exists(APPROVED) else []:
        file_path = os.path.join(APPROVED, file)
        with open(file_path, "r") as f:
            data = json.load(f)
            if data.get("student_id") == str(student_id):
                subject = data.get("subject", "Unknown")
                score = data.get("score") or data.get("grade") or 0
                grades[subject] = score

    if grades:
        subjects_list = list(grades.keys())
        scores = list(grades.values())
        plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))
        plt.bar(subjects_list, scores, color='purple')
        plt.ylim(0, 100)
        plt.title("Grades Overview")
        plt.ylabel("Score (%)")
        plt.show()
    else:
        print("No grades available yet.")

    # --- Top Study Recommendations ---
    print("\n--- Top Study Recommendations ---")
    recs = recommend_next_resources(student_id, subjects)
    if recs:
        for r in recs[:5]:
            print(f"- {r['resource']} ({r['type']}, {r['unread_notes']} unread notes)")
    else:
        print("All resources reviewed! Keep practicing or explore optional topics.")

    # --- Progress Summary ---
    progress_percent = (read_notes / total_notes * 100) if total_notes else 0
    print(f"\nOverall Progress: {progress_percent:.2f}% of notes completed")
```

---

### **2. Features of the Student Dashboard**

1. **Notes Completion Bar Chart** - shows how many notes are read/unread.  
2. **Grades Overview** - visualizes scores per subject.  
3. **Top Study Recommendations** - dynamically suggests next chapters, assignments, or exams.  
4. **Progress Summary** - shows percentage of notes completed overall.  
5. Optional enhancements:
   - Color-coded alerts for low progress or pending assignments.  
   - Clickable charts to jump directly to specific notes or assignments.  
   - Integration with **interactive desktop** so progress updates in real-time.

---

### **3. Example Usage**

```python
if __name__ == "__main__":
    STUDENT_ID = 101
    SUBJECTS = ["Math", "Science", "History"]
    student_dashboard(STUDENT_ID, SUBJECTS)
```

### **1. Interactive Student Dashboard - `interactive_student_dashboard.py`**

Here we'll use **Tkinter** for a lightweight GUI that works cross-platform:

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from research_notebook import load_notes, USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE
from study_recommendations import recommend_next_resources
from board_of_education import APPROVED

class StudentDashboard:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        self.student_id = str(student_id)
        self.subjects = subjects
        self.usage_file = USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE.format(student_id=self.student_id)
        self.usage = self.load_usage()
        self.notes = load_notes(self.student_id)

        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Student Dashboard - ID {self.student_id}")
        self.root.geometry("800x600")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_dashboard()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def load_usage(self):
        if os.path.exists(self.usage_file):
            with open(self.usage_file, "r") as f:
                return json.load(f)
        return {}

    def save_usage(self):
        with open(self.usage_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.usage, f, indent=4)

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Notes Frame
        self.notes_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Notes")
        self.notes_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=10)

        self.notes_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.notes_frame, columns=("title", "status"), show="headings")
        self.notes_tree.heading("title", text="Note Title")
        self.notes_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.notes_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, side="left", padx=5, pady=5)

        # Buttons
        self.mark_read_btn = ttk.Button(self.notes_frame, text="Mark as Read", command=self.mark_note_read)
        self.mark_read_btn.pack(padx=5, pady=5, side="left")

        # Recommendations Frame
        self.rec_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Top Study Recommendations")
        self.rec_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=10)
        self.rec_text = tk.Text(self.rec_frame, height=8)
        self.rec_text.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        # Progress Label
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(self.root, text="Overall Progress: 0%")
        self.progress_label.pack(pady=5)

    def refresh_dashboard(self):
        # Update Notes
        for i in self.notes_tree.get_children():
            self.notes_tree.delete(i)
        for note in self.notes:
            status = "Read" if self.usage.get(str(note['id']), False) else "Unread"
            self.notes_tree.insert("", "end", values=(note['title'], status))

        # Update Recommendations
        self.rec_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        recs = recommend_next_resources(self.student_id, self.subjects)
        if recs:
            for r in recs[:5]:
                self.rec_text.insert(tk.END, f"- {r['resource']} ({r['type']}, {r['unread_notes']} unread notes)\n")
        else:
            self.rec_text.insert(tk.END, "All resources reviewed! Keep practicing or explore optional topics.")

        # Update Progress
        total_notes = len(self.notes)
        read_notes = sum(1 for n in self.notes if self.usage.get(str(n['id']), False))
        progress_percent = (read_notes / total_notes * 100) if total_notes else 0
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Overall Progress: {progress_percent:.2f}%")

    def mark_note_read(self):
        selected = self.notes_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Please select a note to mark as read.")
            return
        for sel in selected:
            note_title = self.notes_tree.item(sel, "values")[0]
            note_obj = next((n for n in self.notes if n['title'] == note_title), None)
            if note_obj:
                self.usage[str(note_obj['id'])] = True
        self.save_usage()
        self.refresh_dashboard()
```

---

### **2. Features**

1. **Interactive Notes Table** - students can select notes and mark them as read.  
2. **Top Study Recommendations** - dynamically updated based on unread notes and subjects.  
3. **Real-time Progress Update** - progress percentage refreshes immediately when a note is marked as read.  
4. **Integrated with existing system** - automatically pulls from the **research notebook** and **recommendation engine**.  
5. Future expansion:
   - Click a note to **open full content or assignment**.  
   - Mark assignments/exams complete in a similar manner.  
   - Graphical charts of grades and progress integrated within the same GUI.

---

### **3. Usage Example**

```python
if __name__ == "__main__":
    STUDENT_ID = 101
    SUBJECTS = ["Math", "Science", "History"]
    dashboard = StudentDashboard(STUDENT_ID, SUBJECTS)
```

### **1. Interactive Dashboard with Charts - `interactive_student_dashboard_charts.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from matplotlib.backends.backend_tkagg import FigureCanvasTkAgg
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from research_notebook import load_notes, USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE
from study_recommendations import recommend_next_resources
from board_of_education import APPROVED

class StudentDashboardCharts:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        self.student_id = str(student_id)
        self.subjects = subjects
        self.usage_file = USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE.format(student_id=self.student_id)
        self.usage = self.load_usage()
        self.notes = load_notes(self.student_id)

        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Student Dashboard - ID {self.student_id}")
        self.root.geometry("1000x700")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_dashboard()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def load_usage(self):
        if os.path.exists(self.usage_file):
            with open(self.usage_file, "r") as f:
                return json.load(f)
        return {}

    def save_usage(self):
        with open(self.usage_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.usage, f, indent=4)

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Notes Frame
        self.notes_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Notes")
        self.notes_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=False, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.notes_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.notes_frame, columns=("title", "status"), show="headings")
        self.notes_tree.heading("title", text="Note Title")
        self.notes_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.notes_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, side="left", padx=5, pady=5)

        self.mark_read_btn = ttk.Button(self.notes_frame, text="Mark as Read", command=self.mark_note_read)
        self.mark_read_btn.pack(padx=5, pady=5, side="left")

        # Recommendations Frame
        self.rec_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Top Study Recommendations")
        self.rec_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=False, padx=10, pady=5)
        self.rec_text = tk.Text(self.rec_frame, height=6)
        self.rec_text.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        # Progress and Charts Frame
        self.charts_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Progress & Grades")
        self.charts_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        # Placeholder frames for charts
        self.figure_notes = plt.Figure(figsize=(4,3))
        self.canvas_notes = FigureCanvasTkAgg(self.figure_notes, master=self.charts_frame)
        self.canvas_notes.get_tk_widget().pack(side="left", fill="both", expand=True)

        self.figure_grades = plt.Figure(figsize=(4,3))
        self.canvas_grades = FigureCanvasTkAgg(self.figure_grades, master=self.charts_frame)
        self.canvas_grades.get_tk_widget().pack(side="right", fill="both", expand=True)

        # Overall progress label
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(self.root, text="Overall Progress: 0%")
        self.progress_label.pack(pady=5)

    def refresh_dashboard(self):
        # --- Update Notes Tree ---
        for i in self.notes_tree.get_children():
            self.notes_tree.delete(i)
        for note in self.notes:
            status = "Read" if self.usage.get(str(note['id']), False) else "Unread"
            self.notes_tree.insert("", "end", values=(note['title'], status))

        # --- Recommendations ---
        self.rec_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        recs = recommend_next_resources(self.student_id, self.subjects)
        if recs:
            for r in recs[:5]:
                self.rec_text.insert(tk.END, f"- {r['resource']} ({r['type']}, {r['unread_notes']} unread notes)\n")
        else:
            self.rec_text.insert(tk.END, "All resources reviewed!")

        # --- Update Notes Completion Chart ---
        read_notes = sum(1 for n in self.notes if self.usage.get(str(n['id']), False))
        unread_notes = len(self.notes) - read_notes
        self.figure_notes.clear()
        ax = self.figure_notes.add_subplot(111)
        ax.bar(["Read Notes", "Unread Notes"], [read_notes, unread_notes], color=['green','red'])
        ax.set_title("Notes Completion")
        self.canvas_notes.draw()

        # --- Update Grades Chart ---
        grades = {}
        for file in os.listdir(APPROVED) if os.path.exists(APPROVED) else []:
            file_path = os.path.join(APPROVED, file)
            with open(file_path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
                if data.get("student_id") == self.student_id:
                    subject = data.get("subject", "Unknown")
                    score = data.get("score") or data.get("grade") or 0
                    grades[subject] = score

        self.figure_grades.clear()
        ax2 = self.figure_grades.add_subplot(111)
        if grades:
            subjects_list = list(grades.keys())
            scores = list(grades.values())
            ax2.bar(subjects_list, scores, color='purple')
            ax2.set_ylim(0,100)
            ax2.set_ylabel("Score (%)")
        ax2.set_title("Grades Overview")
        self.canvas_grades.draw()

        # --- Update Overall Progress ---
        total_notes = len(self.notes)
        progress_percent = (read_notes / total_notes * 100) if total_notes else 0
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Overall Progress: {progress_percent:.2f}%")

    def mark_note_read(self):
        selected = self.notes_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Please select a note to mark as read.")
            return
        for sel in selected:
            note_title = self.notes_tree.item(sel, "values")[0]
            note_obj = next((n for n in self.notes if n['title'] == note_title), None)
            if note_obj:
                self.usage[str(note_obj['id'])] = True
        self.save_usage()
        self.refresh_dashboard()
```

---

### **2. Key Features**

1. **Interactive Notes Table** - mark notes as read; updates charts in real time.  
2. **Top Study Recommendations** - shows dynamic next steps.  
3. **Notes Completion Chart** - live bar chart updated immediately.  
4. **Grades Overview Chart** - shows subject scores dynamically.  
5. **Overall Progress Label** - updated in real time.  
6. **GUI layout** - all features in one window; easy for students to navigate.

- Submit their work, which updates progress and grades automatically.  
- See recommendations adjust in real time based on completion.  

This will create a **fully self-contained, immersive educational simulation**.

### **1. Extend the Interactive Dashboard with Assignments/Exams**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from matplotlib.backends.backend_tkagg import FigureCanvasTkAgg
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from research_notebook import load_notes, USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE
from study_recommendations import recommend_next_resources
from board_of_education import APPROVED

# Mock data for assignments/exams
ASSIGNMENTS = {
    "Math": ["Algebra HW 1", "Geometry Quiz 1"],
    "Science": ["Physics Lab 1", "Chemistry Exam 1"],
    "History": ["Ancient Rome Essay", "Medieval Europe Test"]
}

class StudentDashboardFull:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        self.student_id = str(student_id)
        self.subjects = subjects
        self.usage_file = USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE.format(student_id=self.student_id)
        self.usage = self.load_usage()
        self.notes = load_notes(self.student_id)

        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Student Dashboard - ID {self.student_id}")
        self.root.geometry("1000x800")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_dashboard()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def load_usage(self):
        if os.path.exists(self.usage_file):
            with open(self.usage_file, "r") as f:
                return json.load(f)
        return {}

    def save_usage(self):
        with open(self.usage_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.usage, f, indent=4)

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Notes Frame
        self.notes_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Notes")
        self.notes_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=False, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.notes_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.notes_frame, columns=("title", "status"), show="headings")
        self.notes_tree.heading("title", text="Note Title")
        self.notes_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.notes_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, side="left", padx=5, pady=5)

        self.mark_read_btn = ttk.Button(self.notes_frame, text="Mark as Read", command=self.mark_note_read)
        self.mark_read_btn.pack(padx=5, pady=5, side="left")

        # Assignments/Exams Frame
        self.task_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Assignments / Exams")
        self.task_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=False, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.task_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.task_frame, columns=("task", "subject", "status"), show="headings")
        self.task_tree.heading("task", text="Task")
        self.task_tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.task_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.task_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, side="left", padx=5, pady=5)

        self.complete_task_btn = ttk.Button(self.task_frame, text="Complete Task", command=self.complete_task)
        self.complete_task_btn.pack(padx=5, pady=5, side="left")

        # Recommendations Frame
        self.rec_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Top Study Recommendations")
        self.rec_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=False, padx=10, pady=5)
        self.rec_text = tk.Text(self.rec_frame, height=6)
        self.rec_text.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        # Progress & Charts Frame
        self.charts_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Progress & Grades")
        self.charts_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.figure_notes = plt.Figure(figsize=(4,3))
        self.canvas_notes = FigureCanvasTkAgg(self.figure_notes, master=self.charts_frame)
        self.canvas_notes.get_tk_widget().pack(side="left", fill="both", expand=True)

        self.figure_grades = plt.Figure(figsize=(4,3))
        self.canvas_grades = FigureCanvasTkAgg(self.figure_grades, master=self.charts_frame)
        self.canvas_grades.get_tk_widget().pack(side="right", fill="both", expand=True)

        # Overall Progress Label
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(self.root, text="Overall Progress: 0%")
        self.progress_label.pack(pady=5)

    def refresh_dashboard(self):
        # --- Notes ---
        for i in self.notes_tree.get_children():
            self.notes_tree.delete(i)
        for note in self.notes:
            status = "Read" if self.usage.get(str(note['id']), False) else "Unread"
            self.notes_tree.insert("", "end", values=(note['title'], status))

        # --- Assignments/Exams ---
        for i in self.task_tree.get_children():
            self.task_tree.delete(i)
        for subject, tasks in ASSIGNMENTS.items():
            for task in tasks:
                status = self.usage.get(f"task_{task}", "Incomplete")
                self.task_tree.insert("", "end", values=(task, subject, status))

        # --- Recommendations ---
        self.rec_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        recs = recommend_next_resources(self.student_id, self.subjects)
        if recs:
            for r in recs[:5]:
                self.rec_text.insert(tk.END, f"- {r['resource']} ({r['type']}, {r['unread_notes']} unread notes)\n")
        else:
            self.rec_text.insert(tk.END, "All resources reviewed!")

        # --- Notes Completion Chart ---
        read_notes = sum(1 for n in self.notes if self.usage.get(str(n['id']), False))
        unread_notes = len(self.notes) - read_notes
        self.figure_notes.clear()
        ax = self.figure_notes.add_subplot(111)
        ax.bar(["Read Notes", "Unread Notes"], [read_notes, unread_notes], color=['green','red'])
        ax.set_title("Notes Completion")
        self.canvas_notes.draw()

        # --- Grades Chart ---
        grades = {}
        for file in os.listdir(APPROVED) if os.path.exists(APPROVED) else []:
            file_path = os.path.join(APPROVED, file)
            with open(file_path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
                if data.get("student_id") == self.student_id:
                    subject = data.get("subject", "Unknown")
                    score = data.get("score") or data.get("grade") or 0
                    grades[subject] = score
        self.figure_grades.clear()
        ax2 = self.figure_grades.add_subplot(111)
        if grades:
            subjects_list = list(grades.keys())
            scores = list(grades.values())
            ax2.bar(subjects_list, scores, color='purple')
            ax2.set_ylim(0,100)
            ax2.set_ylabel("Score (%)")
        ax2.set_title("Grades Overview")
        self.canvas_grades.draw()

        # --- Overall Progress ---
        total_notes = len(self.notes)
        progress_percent = (read_notes / total_notes * 100) if total_notes else 0
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Overall Progress: {progress_percent:.2f}%")

    def mark_note_read(self):
        selected = self.notes_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Please select a note to mark as read.")
            return
        for sel in selected:
            note_title = self.notes_tree.item(sel, "values")[0]
            note_obj = next((n for n in self.notes if n['title'] == note_title), None)
            if note_obj:
                self.usage[str(note_obj['id'])] = True
        self.save_usage()
        self.refresh_dashboard()

    def complete_task(self):
        selected = self.task_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Please select a task to complete.")
            return
        for sel in selected:
            task_name = self.task_tree.item(sel, "values")[0]
            self.usage[f"task_{task_name}"] = "Completed"
        self.save_usage()
        self.refresh_dashboard()
```

### **1. Teacher Dashboard - `teacher_dashboard.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from research_notebook import NOTES_DIR, save_note

# Location to store tasks and assignments
TASKS_FILE = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, "tasks.json")
if not os.path.exists(TASKS_FILE):
    with open(TASKS_FILE, "w") as f:
        json.dump({}, f, indent=4)

class TeacherDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Teacher Dashboard")
        self.root.geometry("800x600")

        self.load_tasks()
        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_task_list()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def load_tasks(self):
        with open(TASKS_FILE, "r") as f:
            self.tasks = json.load(f)

    def save_tasks(self):
        with open(TASKS_FILE, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.tasks, f, indent=4)

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.task_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Current Tasks / Assignments")
        self.task_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.task_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.task_frame, columns=("subject","task"), show="headings")
        self.task_tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.task_tree.heading("task", text="Task")
        self.task_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        self.entry_subject = ttk.Entry(self.root)
        self.entry_subject.pack(padx=5, pady=5)
        self.entry_subject.insert(0, "Subject")

        self.entry_task = ttk.Entry(self.root)
        self.entry_task.pack(padx=5, pady=5)
        self.entry_task.insert(0, "Task Name")

        self.add_task_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Add Task", command=self.add_task)
        self.add_task_btn.pack(padx=5, pady=5)

        self.remove_task_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Remove Selected Task", command=self.remove_task)
        self.remove_task_btn.pack(padx=5, pady=5)

    def refresh_task_list(self):
        for i in self.task_tree.get_children():
            self.task_tree.delete(i)
        for subject, task_list in self.tasks.items():
            for t in task_list:
                self.task_tree.insert("", "end", values=(subject, t))

    def add_task(self):
        subject = self.entry_subject.get().strip()
        task = self.entry_task.get().strip()
        if not subject or not task:
            messagebox.showwarning("Missing Info", "Enter both subject and task name.")
            return
        if subject not in self.tasks:
            self.tasks[subject] = []
        self.tasks[subject].append(task)
        self.save_tasks()
        self.refresh_task_list()
        messagebox.showinfo("Task Added", f"Added '{task}' to subject '{subject}'.")

    def remove_task(self):
        selected = self.task_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a task to remove.")
            return
        for sel in selected:
            subject, task_name = self.task_tree.item(sel, "values")
            if subject in self.tasks and task_name in self.tasks[subject]:
                self.tasks[subject].remove(task_name)
        self.save_tasks()
        self.refresh_task_list()
        messagebox.showinfo("Task Removed", "Selected task(s) removed.")
```

### **2. Student Dashboard - Live Updates**

We can modify the student dashboard to **reload tasks periodically** or use a **file watcher**:

```python
import threading
import time

def start_auto_refresh(self, interval=5):
    def refresh_loop():
        while True:
            time.sleep(interval)
            self.load_tasks_from_file()
            self.refresh_dashboard()
    threading.Thread(target=refresh_loop, daemon=True).start()

def load_tasks_from_file(self):
    if os.path.exists(TASKS_FILE):
        with open(TASKS_FILE, "r") as f:
            self.tasks = json.load(f)
```

- This ensures that **any new tasks added by teachers** appear automatically on student dashboards.  
- Students can **complete tasks**, and the dashboard updates **progress and recommendations in real-time**.

### **1. Real-Time Student Research Notebook - `research_notebook_dashboard.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox, filedialog

# Base directories
NOTES_DIR = "student_notes"
if not os.path.exists(NOTES_DIR):
    os.makedirs(NOTES_DIR)

USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, "usage_{student_id}.json")

# Each note stored as JSON: {id, title, subject, content, timestamp, submitted}
def save_note(student_id, note):
    student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
    notes = []
    if os.path.exists(student_file):
        with open(student_file, "r") as f:
            notes = json.load(f)
    # Assign ID if new
    if "id" not in note:
        note["id"] = len(notes) + 1
    notes.append(note)
    with open(student_file, "w") as f:
        json.dump(notes, f, indent=4)

def load_notes(student_id):
    student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
    if os.path.exists(student_file):
        with open(student_file, "r") as f:
            return json.load(f)
    return []

class ResearchNotebook:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        self.student_id = str(student_id)
        self.subjects = subjects
        self.notes = load_notes(self.student_id)
        self.usage_file = USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE.format(student_id=self.student_id)
        self.usage = self.load_usage()

        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Research Notebook - Student {self.student_id}")
        self.root.geometry("900x600")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_notes()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def load_usage(self):
        if os.path.exists(self.usage_file):
            with open(self.usage_file, "r") as f:
                return json.load(f)
        return {}

    def save_usage(self):
        with open(self.usage_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.usage, f, indent=4)

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Notes list
        self.notes_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Your Notes")
        self.notes_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.notes_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.notes_frame, columns=("id","title","subject","status"), show="headings")
        self.notes_tree.heading("id", text="ID")
        self.notes_tree.heading("title", text="Title")
        self.notes_tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.notes_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.notes_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, side="left", padx=5, pady=5)

        self.notes_tree.bind("<Double-1>", self.open_note)

        # Add/Edit Note Button
        self.add_note_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Add New Note", command=self.add_note)
        self.add_note_btn.pack(pady=5)

        # Submit Note Button
        self.submit_note_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Submit Selected Note", command=self.submit_note)
        self.submit_note_btn.pack(pady=5)

    def refresh_notes(self):
        for i in self.notes_tree.get_children():
            self.notes_tree.delete(i)
        self.notes = load_notes(self.student_id)
        for note in self.notes:
            status = "Submitted" if note.get("submitted") else "Draft"
            self.notes_tree.insert("", "end", values=(note["id"], note["title"], note["subject"], status))

    def add_note(self):
        NoteEditor(self.student_id, self.subjects, self.refresh_notes)

    def open_note(self, event):
        selected = self.notes_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            return
        note_id = int(self.notes_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0])
        note_obj = next((n for n in self.notes if n["id"] == note_id), None)
        if note_obj:
            NoteEditor(self.student_id, self.subjects, self.refresh_notes, note_obj)

    def submit_note(self):
        selected = self.notes_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a note to submit.")
            return
        note_id = int(self.notes_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0])
        notes = load_notes(self.student_id)
        for note in notes:
            if note["id"] == note_id:
                note["submitted"] = True
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{self.student_id}.json")
        with open(student_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(notes, f, indent=4)
        messagebox.showinfo("Submitted", f"Note ID {note_id} submitted successfully.")
        self.refresh_notes()

class NoteEditor:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects, refresh_callback, note=None):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.subjects = subjects
        self.note = note
        self.refresh_callback = refresh_callback

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title("Note Editor")
        self.win.geometry("600x400")

        ttk.Label(self.win, text="Title:").pack(pady=2)
        self.entry_title = ttk.Entry(self.win, width=50)
        self.entry_title.pack(pady=2)
        if note:
            self.entry_title.insert(0, note["title"])

        ttk.Label(self.win, text="Subject:").pack(pady=2)
        self.subject_var = tk.StringVar()
        self.subject_combo = ttk.Combobox(self.win, textvariable=self.subject_var, values=self.subjects)
        self.subject_combo.pack(pady=2)
        if note:
            self.subject_combo.set(note["subject"])

        ttk.Label(self.win, text="Content:").pack(pady=2)
        self.text_content = tk.Text(self.win, height=15, width=70)
        self.text_content.pack(pady=5)
        if note:
            self.text_content.insert("1.0", note["content"])

        self.save_btn = ttk.Button(self.win, text="Save Note", command=self.save_note)
        self.save_btn.pack(pady=5)

    def save_note(self):
        title = self.entry_title.get().strip()
        subject = self.subject_var.get().strip()
        content = self.text_content.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not title or not subject or not content:
            messagebox.showwarning("Incomplete", "All fields are required.")
            return
        note_obj = {"title": title, "subject": subject, "content": content}
        if self.note:
            note_obj["id"] = self.note["id"]
            note_obj["submitted"] = self.note.get("submitted", False)
        save_note(self.student_id, note_obj)
        messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Note '{title}' saved successfully.")
        self.refresh_callback()
        self.win.destroy()
```

### **2. Features of the Research Notebook**

2. **Submit Notes for Review** - marks notes as "Submitted" for teacher/BoE review.  
3. **Track Draft vs Submitted Notes** - keeps clear status.  
4. **Subject-linked Notes** - organized by subject for easier study and recommendations.  
5. **Integrated with Student Dashboard** - can connect with progress tracking and recommendations.

```python

    STUDENT_ID = 101
    SUBJECTS = ["Math", "Science", "History"]
    notebook = ResearchNotebook(STUDENT_ID, SUBJECTS)
```

### **1. Teacher/BoE Review Dashboard - `review_dashboard.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from research_notebook import NOTES_DIR

# Base directories
REVIEW_DIR = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, "review_archive")
if not os.path.exists(REVIEW_DIR):
    os.makedirs(REVIEW_DIR)

class ReviewDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Teacher/BoE Review Dashboard")
        self.root.geometry("900x600")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_submissions()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Submissions list
        self.submissions_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Submitted Notes")
        self.submissions_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.submissions_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.submissions_frame,
                                             columns=("student_id","note_id","title","subject","status"),
                                             show="headings")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("student_id", text="Student ID")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("note_id", text="Note ID")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("title", text="Title")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.submissions_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        self.submissions_tree.bind("<Double-1>", self.open_submission)

        # Action buttons
        self.approve_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Approve Note", command=self.approve_note)
        self.approve_btn.pack(pady=5)
        self.comment_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Add Comment", command=self.add_comment)
        self.comment_btn.pack(pady=5)
        self.refresh_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Refresh Submissions", command=self.refresh_submissions)
        self.refresh_btn.pack(pady=5)

    def refresh_submissions(self):
        for i in self.submissions_tree.get_children():
            self.submissions_tree.delete(i)

        # Scan all student notes
        for file in os.listdir(NOTES_DIR):
            if file.startswith("notes_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                student_id = file.split("_")[1].split(".")[0]
                with open(os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    notes = json.load(f)
                for note in notes:
                    if note.get("submitted"):
                        status = note.get("status", "Pending")
                        self.submissions_tree.insert("", "end",
                                                     values=(student_id, note["id"], note["title"], note["subject"], status))

    def open_submission(self, event):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        note_obj = self.load_note(student_id, int(note_id))
        if note_obj:
            NoteReviewWindow(student_id, note_obj, self.refresh_submissions)

    def load_note(self, student_id, note_id):
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
        if os.path.exists(student_file):
            with open(student_file, "r") as f:
                notes = json.load(f)
            for note in notes:
                if note["id"] == note_id:
                    return note
        return None

    def approve_note(self):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a note to approve.")
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
        with open(student_file, "r") as f:
            notes = json.load(f)
        for note in notes:
            if note["id"] == int(note_id):
                note["status"] = "Approved"
                # Archive approved note
                archive_file = os.path.join(REVIEW_DIR, f"{student_id}_{note_id}.json")
                with open(archive_file, "w") as af:
                    json.dump(note, af, indent=4)
        with open(student_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(notes, f, indent=4)
        messagebox.showinfo("Approved", f"Note ID {note_id} approved and archived.")
        self.refresh_submissions()

    def add_comment(self):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a note to comment on.")
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
        with open(student_file, "r") as f:
            notes = json.load(f)
        for note in notes:
            if note["id"] == int(note_id):
                CommentWindow(student_id, note, self.refresh_submissions)
                return

class NoteReviewWindow:
    def __init__(self, student_id, note_obj, refresh_callback):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.note = note_obj
        self.refresh_callback = refresh_callback

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Review Note ID {self.note['id']} - Student {student_id}")
        self.win.geometry("600x400")

        tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Title: {self.note['title']}").pack()
        tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Subject: {self.note['subject']}").pack()

        self.text_content = tk.Text(self.win, height=20, width=70)
        self.text_content.pack()
        self.text_content.insert("1.0", self.note["content"])
        self.text_content.config(state="disabled")

class CommentWindow:
    def __init__(self, student_id, note_obj, refresh_callback):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.note = note_obj
        self.refresh_callback = refresh_callback

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Add Comment to Note ID {self.note['id']}")
        self.win.geometry("400x300")

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Comment:").pack(pady=5)
        self.text_comment = tk.Text(self.win, height=10, width=50)
        self.text_comment.pack(pady=5)

        self.add_btn = ttk.Button(self.win, text="Submit Comment", command=self.save_comment)
        self.add_btn.pack(pady=5)

    def save_comment(self):
        comment = self.text_comment.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not comment:
            messagebox.showwarning("Empty", "Cannot submit empty comment.")
            return
        if "comments" not in self.note:
            self.note["comments"] = []
        self.note["comments"].append(comment)
        # Save back to student file
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{self.student_id}.json")
        with open(student_file, "r") as f:
            notes = json.load(f)
        for n in notes:
            if n["id"] == self.note["id"]:
                n.update(self.note)
        with open(student_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(notes, f, indent=4)
        messagebox.showinfo("Comment Added", "Comment saved successfully.")
        self.refresh_callback()
        self.win.destroy()
```

Perfect - now we'll implement **real-time student updates based on teacher/BoE review actions**. This will close the loop so that:  

- When a **note is approved or commented on**, the student **immediately sees it on their dashboard/notebook**.  
- Students get **live notifications** for approvals, comments, or grading changes.  
- Progress and recommendations **adjust automatically**.  

We can achieve this using a **file-watcher mechanism** for each student, checking the notes directory for changes in **status or comments**.

---

### **1. Real-Time Updates in Student Dashboard**

We'll add a **file monitoring thread** to the `ResearchNotebook` class:

```python
import threading
import time

class ResearchNotebook:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        # ... existing init code ...
        self.start_file_watcher(interval=2)  # check every 2 seconds

    # --- Existing methods here ---

    # --- 1. File watcher for real-time updates ---
    def start_file_watcher(self, interval=2):
        def watcher():
            last_mod_time = 0
            student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{self.student_id}.json")
            while True:
                time.sleep(interval)
                if os.path.exists(student_file):
                    mod_time = os.path.getmtime(student_file)
                    if mod_time != last_mod_time:
                        last_mod_time = mod_time
                        self.refresh_notes()  # refresh the notebook when teacher/BoE updates
                        self.notify_new_review()
        threading.Thread(target=watcher, daemon=True).start()

    # --- 2. Notification for new comments or approval ---
    def notify_new_review(self):
        for note in self.notes:
            status = note.get("status")
            comments = note.get("comments", [])
            if status == "Approved" and not self.usage.get(f"notified_approved_{note['id']}", False):
                self.usage[f"notified_approved_{note['id']}"] = True
                self.save_usage()
                messagebox.showinfo("Note Approved", f"Your note '{note['title']}' has been approved!")

            for idx, c in enumerate(comments):
                comment_flag = f"notified_comment_{note['id']}_{idx}"
                if not self.usage.get(comment_flag, False):
                    self.usage[comment_flag] = True
                    self.save_usage()
                    messagebox.showinfo("New Comment", f"New comment on '{note['title']}':\n{c}")
```

---

### **2. How it Works**

1. **File Watcher Thread** - checks the student notes file every 2 seconds.  
2. **Detect Changes** - compares modification timestamps to reload notes.  
3. **Notifications** - pops up alerts when a note is:  
   - Approved  
   - Received a new comment  
4. **Usage Flags** - ensures the student only sees each notification **once**.  
5. **Auto-Refresh** - updates the research notebook and dashboard with the latest statuses.  

---

### **3. Optional Integration with Dashboard Progress**

You can extend this to automatically **update progress charts or study recommendations** whenever a note is approved or commented on:

```python
def notify_new_review(self):
    updated = False
    for note in self.notes:
        # Approvals
        if note.get("status") == "Approved" and not self.usage.get(f"notified_approved_{note['id']}", False):
            self.usage[f"notified_approved_{note['id']}"] = True
            updated = True
            messagebox.showinfo("Note Approved", f"Your note '{note['title']}' has been approved!")
        # Comments
        for idx, c in enumerate(note.get("comments", [])):
            comment_flag = f"notified_comment_{note['id']}_{idx}"
            if not self.usage.get(comment_flag, False):
                self.usage[comment_flag] = True
                updated = True
                messagebox.showinfo("New Comment", f"New comment on '{note['title']}':\n{c}")
    if updated:
        self.refresh_dashboard()  # update charts/recommendations if needed
        self.save_usage()
```

### **1. BoE QA Dashboard - `boe_dashboard.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from research_notebook import NOTES_DIR, USAGE_FILE_TEMPLATE

# Directory to archive reviewed submissions
BOE_ARCHIVE = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, "boe_archive")
if not os.path.exists(BOE_ARCHIVE):
    os.makedirs(BOE_ARCHIVE)

class BoEDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("BoE QA Dashboard")
        self.root.geometry("1000x600")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.refresh_all_submissions()
        self.start_auto_refresh(interval=5)
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Students tree
        self.tree_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="All Student Submissions")
        self.tree_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.submissions_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.tree_frame,
                                             columns=("student_id","note_id","title","subject","status"),
                                             show="headings")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("student_id", text="Student ID")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("note_id", text="Note ID")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("title", text="Title")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.submissions_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.submissions_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        self.submissions_tree.bind("<Double-1>", self.open_submission)

        # Action buttons
        self.approve_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Approve Submission", command=self.approve_submission)
        self.approve_btn.pack(pady=5)
        self.comment_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Add Comment", command=self.add_comment)
        self.comment_btn.pack(pady=5)
        self.flag_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Flag for Review", command=self.flag_submission)
        self.flag_btn.pack(pady=5)

    # --- Load all submissions ---
    def refresh_all_submissions(self):
        for i in self.submissions_tree.get_children():
            self.submissions_tree.delete(i)

        for file in os.listdir(NOTES_DIR):
            if file.startswith("notes_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                student_id = file.split("_")[1].split(".")[0]
                with open(os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    notes = json.load(f)
                for note in notes:
                    status = note.get("status", "Pending")
                    if note.get("submitted"):
                        self.submissions_tree.insert("", "end",
                                                     values=(student_id, note["id"], note["title"], note["subject"], status))

    # --- Open submission for review ---
    def open_submission(self, event):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        note_obj = self.load_note(student_id, int(note_id))
        if note_obj:
            SubmissionReviewWindow(student_id, note_obj, self.refresh_all_submissions)

    def load_note(self, student_id, note_id):
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
        if os.path.exists(student_file):
            with open(student_file, "r") as f:
                notes = json.load(f)
            for note in notes:
                if note["id"] == note_id:
                    return note
        return None

    # --- Approve submission ---
    def approve_submission(self):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a submission to approve.")
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        self.update_status(student_id, int(note_id), "Approved")

    # --- Flag submission ---
    def flag_submission(self):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a submission to flag.")
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        self.update_status(student_id, int(note_id), "Flagged")

    # --- Add comment ---
    def add_comment(self):
        selected = self.submissions_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("No Selection", "Select a submission to comment on.")
            return
        student_id, note_id = self.submissions_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0:2]
        note_obj = self.load_note(student_id, int(note_id))
        if note_obj:
            CommentWindow(student_id, note_obj, self.refresh_all_submissions)

    # --- Helper to update status ---
    def update_status(self, student_id, note_id, status):
        student_file = os.path.join(NOTES_DIR, f"notes_{student_id}.json")
        with open(student_file, "r") as f:
            notes = json.load(f)
        for note in notes:
            if note["id"] == note_id:
                note["status"] = status
                archive_file = os.path.join(BOE_ARCHIVE, f"{student_id}_{note_id}.json")
                with open(archive_file, "w") as af:
                    json.dump(note, af, indent=4)
        with open(student_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(notes, f, indent=4)
        messagebox.showinfo("Updated", f"Submission ID {note_id} status set to {status}.")
        self.refresh_all_submissions()

    # --- Auto-refresh for real-time monitoring ---
    def start_auto_refresh(self, interval=5):
        def refresh_loop():
            while True:
                time.sleep(interval)
                self.refresh_all_submissions()
        import threading
        threading.Thread(target=refresh_loop, daemon=True).start()

# --- Review Window ---
class SubmissionReviewWindow:
    def __init__(self, student_id, note_obj, refresh_callback):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.note = note_obj
        self.refresh_callback = refresh_callback

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Review Submission {self.note['id']} - Student {student_id}")
        self.win.geometry("600x400")

        tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Title: {self.note['title']}").pack()
        tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Subject: {self.note['subject']}").pack()

        self.text_content = tk.Text(self.win, height=20, width=70)
        self.text_content.pack()
        self.text_content.insert("1.0", self.note["content"])
        self.text_content.config(state="disabled")

# --- Comment Window ---
class CommentWindow:
    def __init__(self, student_id, note_obj, refresh_callback):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.note = note_obj
        self.refresh_callback = refresh_callback

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Add Comment to Submission {self.note['id']}")
        self.win.geometry("400x300")

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Comment:").pack(pady=5)
        self.text_comment = tk.Text(self.win, height=10, width=50)
        self.text_comment.pack(pady=5)

        self.add_btn = ttk.Button(self.win, text="Submit Comment", command=self.save_comment)
        self.add_btn.pack(pady=5)

    def save_comment(self):
        comment = self.text_comment.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not comment:
            messagebox.showwarning("Empty", "Cannot submit empty comment.")
            return
        if "comments" not in self.note:
            self.note["comments"] = []
        self.note["comments"].append(comment)
        # Save back to student file

                n.update(self.note)

            json.dump(notes, f, indent=4)
        messagebox.showinfo("Comment Added", "Comment saved successfully.")
        self.refresh_callback()
        self.win.destroy()
```

### **2. Main Entry - `main.py`**

```python
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from student.dashboard import ResearchNotebook
from teacher.teacher_dashboard import TeacherDashboard
from boe.boe_dashboard import BoEDashboard

def launch_app():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("Academy OS")
    root.geometry("400x300")

    tk.Label(root, text="Select Role:").pack(pady=20)

    tk.Button(root, text="Student", width=20, command=launch_student).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(root, text="Teacher", width=20, command=launch_teacher).pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(root, text="BoE", width=20, command=launch_boe).pack(pady=5)

    root.mainloop()

def launch_student():
    def start():
        student_id = student_id_entry.get().strip()
        if not student_id.isdigit():
            messagebox.showwarning("Invalid ID", "Student ID must be a number.")
            return
        subjects = ["Math", "Science", "History", "English"]
        student_win.destroy()
        ResearchNotebook(student_id, subjects)

    student_win = tk.Toplevel()
    student_win.title("Student Login")
    tk.Label(student_win, text="Enter Student ID:").pack(pady=5)
    student_id_entry = tk.Entry(student_win)
    student_id_entry.pack(pady=5)
    tk.Button(student_win, text="Start", command=start).pack(pady=5)

def launch_teacher():
    TeacherDashboard()

def launch_boe():
    BoEDashboard()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    launch_app()
```

### **1. Procedural Assignment Generator - `assignment_generator.py`**

```python
import json
import random
import os
from datetime import datetime

ASSIGNMENTS_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
if not os.path.exists(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
    os.makedirs(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR)

# Example question banks
QUESTION_BANK = {
    "Math": [
        {"type": "mcq", "question": "What is 7 + 5?", "options": ["10","11","12","13"], "answer": "12"},
        {"type": "mcq", "question": "Solve for x: 2x=10", "options": ["2","5","10","20"], "answer": "5"},
        {"type": "short", "question": "Integrate x dx", "answer": "0.5*x^2 + C"}
    ],
    "Science": [
        {"type": "mcq", "question": "Water's chemical formula?", "options": ["H2O","CO2","O2","H2"], "answer": "H2O"},
        {"type": "short", "question": "State Newton's second law.", "answer": "F = m * a"}
    ],
    "History": [
        {"type": "mcq", "question": "Who discovered America?", "options": ["Columbus","Vespucci","Magellan","Cook"], "answer": "Columbus"},
        {"type": "short", "question": "Year the Berlin Wall fell?", "answer": "1989"}
    ]
}

def generate_assignment(student_id, subject, num_questions=3):
    questions = random.sample(QUESTION_BANK[subject], k=min(num_questions, len(QUESTION_BANK[subject])))
    assignment_id = f"{student_id}_{subject}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
    assignment = {
        "id": assignment_id,
        "student_id": student_id,
        "subject": subject,
        "questions": questions,
        "submitted": False,
        "graded": False,
        "score": None,
        "comments": []
    }

    # Save assignment file
    file_path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, f"{assignment_id}.json")
    with open(file_path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(assignment, f, indent=4)

    return assignment

# --- Automatic grading ---
def grade_assignment(assignment_file):
    with open(assignment_file, "r") as f:
        assignment = json.load(f)

    score = 0
    total = 0
    for q in assignment["questions"]:
        if q["type"] == "mcq":
            total += 1
            student_answer = q.get("student_answer")
            if student_answer and student_answer == q["answer"]:
                score += 1
        # Short answers can be graded manually or using keywords

    assignment["score"] = score
    assignment["graded"] = True

    with open(assignment_file, "w") as f:
        json.dump(assignment, f, indent=4)

    return score, total
```

### **2. Features**

1. **Procedural Generation**  
   - Questions sampled randomly from a bank.  
   - Each student gets **unique sets**.  

2. **Assignment File**  
   - Stored as JSON in `student_resources/assignments`.  
   - Tracks **submission, grading, comments**.  

3. **Automatic Grading**  
   - Grades multiple-choice automatically.  
   - Short-answer/essay can be **reviewed by teachers or BoE**.  

4. **Integration with Dashboards**  
   - Student dashboard shows **new assignments**.  
   - Teachers can **review, grade, and comment**.  
   - BoE sees all submissions for QA.

```python
# Generate assignment for a student
assignment = generate_assignment(student_id=101, subject="Math", num_questions=3)
print("Generated Assignment:", assignment["id"])

# Assume student answers
assignment_file = f"student/student_resources/assignments/{assignment['id']}.json"
with open(assignment_file, "r") as f:
    a = json.load(f)
# Simulate answers
for q in a["questions"]:
    if q["type"] == "mcq":
        q["student_answer"] = random.choice(q["options"])
with open(assignment_file, "w") as f:
    json.dump(a, f, indent=4)

# Grade assignment
score, total = grade_assignment(assignment_file)
print(f"Score: {score}/{total}")
```

### **1. Student Dashboard Assignment Integration**

Add this to the **`ResearchNotebook` class** (or the student dashboard module):

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from core.file_watcher import start_file_watcher  # optional shared utility
from student.assignment_generator import ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, grade_assignment

class ResearchNotebook:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.subjects = subjects
        self.notes = []
        self.assignments = []
        self.usage = {}  # tracking notifications
        self.load_assignments()
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Student Dashboard - ID {self.student_id}")
        self.root.geometry("900x600")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.start_file_watcher(interval=2)
        self.root.mainloop()

    # ------------------ Load assignments ------------------
    def load_assignments(self):
        self.assignments = []
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    self.assignments.append(json.load(f))

    # ------------------ Dashboard GUI ------------------
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Assignments frame
        self.assign_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Assignments & Exams")
        self.assign_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.assign_tree = ttk.Treeview(self.assign_frame,
                                        columns=("id","subject","status","score"),
                                        show="headings")
        self.assign_tree.heading("id", text="Assignment ID")
        self.assign_tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.assign_tree.heading("status", text="Status")
        self.assign_tree.heading("score", text="Score")
        self.assign_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        self.assign_tree.bind("<Double-1>", self.open_assignment)

        # Refresh button
        self.refresh_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Refresh Assignments", command=self.refresh_assignments)
        self.refresh_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.refresh_assignments()

    # ------------------ Refresh assignment list ------------------
    def refresh_assignments(self):
        for i in self.assign_tree.get_children():
            self.assign_tree.delete(i)
        self.load_assignments()
        for a in self.assignments:
            status = "Submitted" if a.get("submitted") else "Pending"
            score = a.get("score") if a.get("graded") else "-"
            self.assign_tree.insert("", "end",
                                    values=(a["id"], a["subject"], status, score))

    # ------------------ Open assignment for answering ------------------
    def open_assignment(self, event):
        selected = self.assign_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            return
        assignment_id = self.assign_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0]
        assignment = next((a for a in self.assignments if a["id"] == assignment_id), None)
        if assignment:
            AssignmentWindow(self, assignment)

    # ------------------ File watcher for real-time updates ------------------
    def start_file_watcher(self, interval=2):
        import threading
        import time
        def watcher():
            last_mod_times = {}
            while True:
                time.sleep(interval)
                updated = False
                for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
                    if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                        path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file)
                        mod_time = os.path.getmtime(path)
                        if path not in last_mod_times or last_mod_times[path] != mod_time:
                            last_mod_times[path] = mod_time
                            updated = True
                if updated:
                    self.refresh_assignments()
                    self.notify_new_grades()

        threading.Thread(target=watcher, daemon=True).start()

    # ------------------ Notifications for graded assignments ------------------
    def notify_new_grades(self):
        for a in self.assignments:
            if a.get("graded") and not self.usage.get(f"notified_grade_{a['id']}", False):
                self.usage[f"notified_grade_{a['id']}"] = True
                messagebox.showinfo("Assignment Graded", f"{a['subject']} - {a['id']} graded: Score {a['score']}")
```

### **2. Assignment Answering Window**

```python
class AssignmentWindow:
    def __init__(self, dashboard, assignment):
        self.dashboard = dashboard
        self.assignment = assignment

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Assignment: {assignment['id']}")
        self.win.geometry("600x500")

        self.entries = []

        # Display questions
        for idx, q in enumerate(assignment["questions"]):
            tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Q{idx+1}: {q['question']}").pack(pady=2)
            if q["type"] == "mcq":
                var = tk.StringVar()
                for opt in q["options"]:
                    tk.Radiobutton(self.win, text=opt, variable=var, value=opt).pack(anchor="w")
                self.entries.append((q, var))
            else:  # short/essay
                text_entry = tk.Text(self.win, height=3, width=50)
                text_entry.pack(pady=2)
                self.entries.append((q, text_entry))

        # Submit button
        tk.Button(self.win, text="Submit Assignment", command=self.submit_assignment).pack(pady=10)

    def submit_assignment(self):
        # Record answers
        for q, widget in self.entries:
            if q["type"] == "mcq":
                q["student_answer"] = widget.get()
            else:
                q["student_answer"] = widget.get("1.0", "end").strip()
        self.assignment["submitted"] = True

        # Save back to file
        file_path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, f"{self.assignment['id']}.json")
        with open(file_path, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.assignment, f, indent=4)

        messagebox.showinfo("Submitted", f"Assignment {self.assignment['id']} submitted successfully.")
        self.dashboard.refresh_assignments()
        self.win.destroy()
```

### **1. Procedural Exam Generator - `exam_generator.py`**

```python
import json
import random
import os
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

EXAMS_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"
if not os.path.exists(EXAMS_DIR):
    os.makedirs(EXAMS_DIR)

# Question banks (can extend with more subjects)
EXAM_QUESTION_BANK = {
    "Math": [
        {"type":"mcq","question":"5*6=?","options":["28","30","32","35"],"answer":"30"},
        {"type":"mcq","question":"Solve x: 2x+4=12","options":["3","4","6","8"],"answer":"4"},
        {"type":"short","question":"Integrate 2x dx","answer":"x^2 + C"}
    ],
    "Science": [
        {"type":"mcq","question":"H2O is?","options":["Water","Oxygen","Hydrogen","CO2"],"answer":"Water"},
        {"type":"short","question":"State Newton's 1st law","answer":"Inertia"}
    ]
}

def generate_exam(student_id, subject, num_questions=5, duration_minutes=30):
    questions = random.sample(EXAM_QUESTION_BANK[subject], k=min(num_questions, len(EXAM_QUESTION_BANK[subject])))
    exam_id = f"{student_id}_{subject}_EXAM_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
    exam = {
        "id": exam_id,
        "student_id": student_id,
        "subject": subject,
        "questions": questions,
        "submitted": False,
        "graded": False,
        "score": None,
        "comments": [],
        "duration_minutes": duration_minutes,
        "start_time": None
    }

    # Save exam file
    file_path = os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, f"{exam_id}.json")
    with open(file_path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(exam, f, indent=4)

    return exam

# ----------------- Automatic grading -----------------
def grade_exam(exam_file):
    with open(exam_file, "r") as f:
        exam = json.load(f)

    score = 0
    total = 0
    for q in exam["questions"]:
        if q["type"] == "mcq":
            total += 1
            student_answer = q.get("student_answer")
            if student_answer and student_answer == q["answer"]:
                score += 1
        # Short answers can be graded manually or using keyword matching

    exam["score"] = score
    exam["graded"] = True

    with open(exam_file, "w") as f:
        json.dump(exam, f, indent=4)

    return score, total
```

```python
    # ------------------ Exams GUI ------------------
    def create_exam_tab(self):

    def open_exam(self, event):
        selected = self.exam_tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            return
        exam_id = self.exam_tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0]
        exam = next((e for e in self.exams if e["id"] == exam_id), None)
        if exam:
            ExamWindow(self, exam)
```

### **3. Exam Taking Window (with Timer)**

```python
import threading
import time

class ExamWindow:
    def __init__(self, dashboard, exam):
        self.dashboard = dashboard
        self.exam = exam
        self.time_left = exam["duration_minutes"] * 60
        self.entries = []

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Exam: {exam['id']}")
        self.win.geometry("700x600")

        self.timer_label = tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Time left: {self.time_left//60}m {self.time_left%60}s")
        self.timer_label.pack(pady=5)

        # Questions
        for idx, q in enumerate(exam["questions"]):
            tk.Label(self.win, text=f"Q{idx+1}: {q['question']}").pack(pady=2)
            if q["type"] == "mcq":
                var = tk.StringVar()
                for opt in q["options"]:
                    tk.Radiobutton(self.win, text=opt, variable=var, value=opt).pack(anchor="w")
                self.entries.append((q, var))
            else:
                text_entry = tk.Text(self.win, height=3, width=60)
                text_entry.pack(pady=2)
                self.entries.append((q, text_entry))

        tk.Button(self.win, text="Submit Exam", command=self.submit_exam).pack(pady=10)

        # Start countdown timer
        threading.Thread(target=self.countdown_timer, daemon=True).start()

    def countdown_timer(self):
        while self.time_left > 0:
            time.sleep(1)
            self.time_left -= 1
            self.timer_label.config(text=f"Time left: {self.time_left//60}m {self.time_left%60}s")
        if not self.exam.get("submitted"):
            messagebox.showinfo("Time Up", "Exam time is over. Submitting automatically.")
            self.submit_exam()

    def submit_exam(self):
        # Record answers
        for q, widget in self.entries:
            if q["type"] == "mcq":
                q["student_answer"] = widget.get()
            else:
                q["student_answer"] = widget.get("1.0", "end").strip()
        self.exam["submitted"] = True

        # Save exam
        file_path = os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, f"{self.exam['id']}.json")
        with open(file_path, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.exam, f, indent=4)

        messagebox.showinfo("Submitted", f"Exam {self.exam['id']} submitted successfully.")
        self.dashboard.refresh_exams()
        self.win.destroy()
```

### **1. Analytics Module - `analytics.py`**

```python
import os
import json

ASSIGNMENTS_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAMS_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"

def load_student_results(student_id):
    results = []
    # Load assignments
    for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
        if file.startswith(f"{student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
            with open(os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                results.append(json.load(f))
    # Load exams
    for file in os.listdir(EXAMS_DIR):
        if file.startswith(f"{student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
            with open(os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                results.append(json.load(f))
    return results

def calculate_performance(student_id):
    results = load_student_results(student_id)
    subject_scores = {}
    subject_counts = {}

    for item in results:
        if not item.get("graded") or item.get("score") is None:
            continue
        subj = item["subject"]
        subject_scores[subj] = subject_scores.get(subj, 0) + item["score"]
        subject_counts[subj] = subject_counts.get(subj, 0) + len(item["questions"])

    # Average per subject
    avg_scores = {}
    for subj in subject_scores:
        avg_scores[subj] = round(subject_scores[subj] / subject_counts[subj] * 100, 2)
    return avg_scores

def generate_recommendations(student_id):
    avg_scores = calculate_performance(student_id)
    recommendations = {}
    for subj, score in avg_scores.items():
        if score >= 85:
            recommendations[subj] = "Keep up the excellent work. Explore advanced exercises."
        elif score >= 65:
            recommendations[subj] = "Moderate performance. Review key topics and practice more."
        else:
            recommendations[subj] = "Low performance. Focus on foundational concepts and exercises."
    return avg_scores, recommendations
```

### **2. Integrate Analytics into Student Dashboard**

Add an **Analytics Tab** to the `ResearchNotebook`:

```python
from analytics import generate_recommendations

class ResearchNotebook:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        # ... existing init ...
        self.create_analytics_tab()

    def create_analytics_tab(self):
        self.analytics_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Performance Analytics & Recommendations")
        self.analytics_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.analytics_text = tk.Text(self.analytics_frame, height=15, width=100)
        self.analytics_text.pack(padx=5, pady=5)
        self.update_analytics()

    def update_analytics(self):
        self.analytics_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        avg_scores, recommendations = generate_recommendations(self.student_id)
        self.analytics_text.insert(tk.END, "=== Subject Performance ===\n")
        for subj, score in avg_scores.items():
            self.analytics_text.insert(tk.END, f"{subj}: {score}%\n")
        self.analytics_text.insert(tk.END, "\n=== Recommendations ===\n")
        for subj, rec in recommendations.items():
            self.analytics_text.insert(tk.END, f"{subj}: {rec}\n")
```

### **1. Teacher & BoE Analytics Module - `admin_analytics.py`**

```python
import os
import json

ASSIGNMENTS_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAMS_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"

def load_all_student_results():
    results = {}
    # Load assignments
    for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
        if file.endswith(".json"):
            with open(os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                a = json.load(f)
                sid = a["student_id"]
                results[sid] = results.get(sid, []) + [a]
    # Load exams
    for file in os.listdir(EXAMS_DIR):
        if file.endswith(".json"):
            with open(os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                e = json.load(f)
                sid = e["student_id"]
                results[sid] = results.get(sid, []) + [e]
    return results

def compute_class_analytics():
    all_results = load_all_student_results()
    class_scores = {}
    student_summaries = {}

    for sid, items in all_results.items():
        subj_scores = {}
        subj_counts = {}
        for item in items:
            if not item.get("graded") or item.get("score") is None:
                continue
            subj = item["subject"]
            subj_scores[subj] = subj_scores.get(subj, 0) + item["score"]
            subj_counts[subj] = subj_counts.get(subj, 0) + len(item["questions"])
        avg_scores = {subj: round(subj_scores[subj] / subj_counts[subj] * 100, 2) for subj in subj_scores}
        student_summaries[sid] = avg_scores

        for subj, score in avg_scores.items():
            class_scores[subj] = class_scores.get(subj, []) + [score]

    # Compute class averages per subject
    class_avg = {subj: round(sum(scores)/len(scores),2) for subj, scores in class_scores.items()}

    return class_avg, student_summaries
```

### **2. Teacher Analytics Dashboard Integration**

```python
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from admin_analytics import compute_class_analytics

class TeacherDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Teacher Dashboard")
        self.root.geometry("900x600")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.analytics_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Class Analytics & QA")
        self.analytics_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(self.analytics_frame,
                                 columns=("student_id","subject","score"),
                                 show="headings")
        self.tree.heading("student_id", text="Student ID")
        self.tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.tree.heading("score", text="Score (%)")
        self.tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        self.refresh_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Refresh Analytics", command=self.refresh_analytics)
        self.refresh_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.refresh_analytics()

    def refresh_analytics(self):
        for i in self.tree.get_children():
            self.tree.delete(i)
        class_avg, student_summaries = compute_class_analytics()
        for sid, subj_scores in student_summaries.items():
            for subj, score in subj_scores.items():
                self.tree.insert("", "end", values=(sid, subj, score))
        avg_str = ", ".join([f"{subj}: {avg}%" for subj, avg in class_avg.items()])
        messagebox.showinfo("Class Averages", f"Class average per subject:\n{avg_str}")
```

### **3. BoE Dashboard Integration**
