```python
class BoEDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Board of Education Dashboard")
        self.root.geometry("1000x600")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.analytics_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="School-wide Performance & QA")
        self.analytics_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(self.analytics_frame,
                                 columns=("student_id","subject","score","graded","comments"),
                                 show="headings")
        self.tree.heading("student_id", text="Student ID")
        self.tree.heading("subject", text="Subject")
        self.tree.heading("score", text="Score (%)")
        self.tree.heading("graded", text="Graded")
        self.tree.heading("comments", text="Teacher Comments")
        self.tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)

        self.refresh_btn = ttk.Button(self.root, text="Refresh Analytics", command=self.refresh_analytics)
        self.refresh_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.refresh_analytics()

    def refresh_analytics(self):
        from admin_analytics import load_all_student_results
        for i in self.tree.get_children():
            self.tree.delete(i)

        all_results = load_all_student_results()
        for sid, items in all_results.items():
            for item in items:
                score = item.get("score") if item.get("graded") else "-"
                graded = item.get("graded")
                comments = "; ".join(item.get("comments", []))
                self.tree.insert("", "end", values=(sid, item["subject"], score, graded, comments))
```

### **1. Notification Manager - `notifications.py`**

```python
import os
import json
from datetime import datetime

ASSIGNMENTS_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAMS_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"

class NotificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.notified = {}  # track which alerts were already shown

    def check_student_notifications(self, student_id):
        notifications = []
        # Check assignments
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    a = json.load(f)
                key = f"assignment_{a['id']}_grade"
                if a.get("graded") and key not in self.notified:
                    notifications.append(f"Assignment graded: {a['subject']} - {a['id']} (Score: {a['score']})")
                    self.notified[key] = True

        # Check exams
        for file in os.listdir(EXAMS_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    e = json.load(f)
                key = f"exam_{e['id']}_grade"
                if e.get("graded") and key not in self.notified:
                    notifications.append(f"Exam graded: {e['subject']} - {e['id']} (Score: {e['score']})")
                    self.notified[key] = True

        return notifications

    def check_teacher_notifications(self):
        notifications = []
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
            if file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    a = json.load(f)
                key = f"teacher_{a['id']}_submit"
                if a.get("submitted") and not a.get("graded") and key not in self.notified:
                    notifications.append(f"Assignment submitted: Student {a['student_id']} - {a['subject']} ({a['id']})")
                    self.notified[key] = True
        for file in os.listdir(EXAMS_DIR):
            if file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    e = json.load(f)
                key = f"teacher_{e['id']}_submit"
                if e.get("submitted") and not e.get("graded") and key not in self.notified:
                    notifications.append(f"Exam submitted: Student {e['student_id']} - {e['subject']} ({e['id']})")
                    self.notified[key] = True
        return notifications

    def check_boe_notifications(self):
        notifications = []
        # Flag assignments/exams not graded within 48 hours
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
            if file.endswith(".json"):
                path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file)
                with open(path, "r") as f:
                    a = json.load(f)
                key = f"boe_{a['id']}_late"
                if a.get("submitted") and not a.get("graded"):
                    submit_time = datetime.strptime(a.get("id").split("_")[-1], "%Y%m%d%H%M%S")
                    delta = datetime.now() - submit_time
                    if delta.total_seconds() > 48*3600 and key not in self.notified:
                        notifications.append(f"Late grading detected: Assignment {a['id']} (Student {a['student_id']})")
                        self.notified[key] = True
        return notifications
```

### **2. Integration into Dashboards**

**Student Dashboard:**  

```python
from notifications import NotificationManager
import threading
import time
from tkinter import messagebox

class ResearchNotebook:
    def __init__(self, student_id, subjects):
        # ... existing init ...
        self.notifications = NotificationManager()
        threading.Thread(target=self.student_notification_loop, daemon=True).start()

    def student_notification_loop(self):
        while True:
            time.sleep(5)  # check every 5 seconds
            notes = self.notifications.check_student_notifications(self.student_id)
            for n in notes:
                messagebox.showinfo("Notification", n)
```

class TeacherDashboard:

        self.notifications = NotificationManager()
        threading.Thread(target=self.teacher_notification_loop, daemon=True).start()

    def teacher_notification_loop(self):
        import time
        while True:
            time.sleep(5)
            notes = self.notifications.check_teacher_notifications()
            for n in notes:
                messagebox.showinfo("Notification", n)
```

        self.notifications = NotificationManager()
        threading.Thread(target=self.boe_notification_loop, daemon=True).start()

    def boe_notification_loop(self):
        import time
        while True:
            time.sleep(60)  # check every minute

### **1. Research Notebook - Core Module (`research_notebook.py`)**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox

NOTEBOOK_DIR = "student/student_resources/notes"
if not os.path.exists(NOTEBOOK_DIR):
    os.makedirs(NOTEBOOK_DIR)

class ResearchNotebook:
    def __init__(self, student_id):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.notes = {}
        self.load_notes()

        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Research Notebook - Student {self.student_id}")
        self.root.geometry("900x600")

        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    # ------------------ Load saved notes ------------------
    def load_notes(self):
        self.notes = {}
        for file in os.listdir(NOTEBOOK_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(NOTEBOOK_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    note = json.load(f)
                    self.notes[note["title"]] = note

    # ------------------ GUI ------------------
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Notes list
        self.notes_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(self.root, text="Saved Research Notes")
        self.notes_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)

        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(self.notes_frame, columns=("title","date"), show="headings")
        self.tree.heading("title", text="Title")
        self.tree.heading("date", text="Last Modified")
        self.tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)
        self.tree.bind("<Double-1>", self.open_note)

        # Buttons
        button_frame = ttk.Frame(self.root)
        button_frame.pack(pady=5)

        ttk.Button(button_frame, text="New Note", command=self.new_note).pack(side="left", padx=5)
        ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Refresh", command=self.refresh_notes).pack(side="left", padx=5)
        ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Delete Note", command=self.delete_note).pack(side="left", padx=5)

        self.refresh_notes()

    # ------------------ Create a new note ------------------
    def new_note(self):
        NoteWindow(self, title="New Note")

    # ------------------ Open existing note ------------------
    def open_note(self, event):
        selected = self.tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            return
        title = self.tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0]
        note = self.notes.get(title)
        if note:
            NoteWindow(self, note)

    # ------------------ Refresh note list ------------------
    def refresh_notes(self):
        for i in self.tree.get_children():
            self.tree.delete(i)
        self.load_notes()
        for title, note in self.notes.items():
            self.tree.insert("", "end", values=(title, note["last_modified"]))

    # ------------------ Delete note ------------------
    def delete_note(self):
        selected = self.tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("Delete Note", "Select a note first.")
            return
        title = self.tree.item(selected[0], "values")[0]
        path = os.path.join(NOTEBOOK_DIR, f"{self.student_id}_{title}.json")
        if os.path.exists(path):
            os.remove(path)
        self.refresh_notes()
```

### **2. Individual Note Window (`NoteWindow`)**

```python
from datetime import datetime

class NoteWindow:
    def __init__(self, notebook, note=None, title=None):
        self.notebook = notebook
        self.note = note
        self.title = title if title else (note["title"] if note else "New Note")

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Research Note - {self.title}")
        self.win.geometry("700x500")

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Title:").pack()
        self.title_entry = tk.Entry(self.win, width=60)
        self.title_entry.pack()
        self.title_entry.insert(0, self.title)

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Content:").pack()
        self.text_area = tk.Text(self.win, height=20, width=80)
        self.text_area.pack()
        if note:
            self.text_area.insert("1.0", note["content"])

        tk.Button(self.win, text="Save Note", command=self.save_note).pack(pady=5)

    def save_note(self):
        title = self.title_entry.get().strip()
        content = self.text_area.get("1.0", "end").strip()
        if not title:
            messagebox.showwarning("Save Note", "Title cannot be empty.")
            return

        note_data = {
            "title": title,
            "content": content,
            "last_modified": datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
            "student_id": self.notebook.student_id
        }

        path = os.path.join(NOTEBOOK_DIR, f"{self.notebook.student_id}_{title}.json")
        with open(path, "w") as f:
            json.dump(note_data, f, indent=4)

        self.notebook.refresh_notes()
        self.win.destroy()
```

### **2. Update `NoteWindow` to Link Notes**

```python
class NoteWindow:
    def __init__(self, notebook, note=None, title=None, link_options=None):
        self.notebook = notebook
        self.note = note
        self.title = title if title else (note["title"] if note else "New Note")
        self.link_options = link_options if link_options else self.get_linkable_items()
        
        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Research Note - {self.title}")
        self.win.geometry("700x600")

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Title:").pack()
        self.title_entry = tk.Entry(self.win, width=60)
        self.title_entry.pack()
        self.title_entry.insert(0, self.title)

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Content:").pack()
        self.text_area = tk.Text(self.win, height=20, width=80)
        self.text_area.pack()
        if note:
            self.text_area.insert("1.0", note["content"])

        # ---------------- Link to assignments/exams ----------------
        tk.Label(self.win, text="Link to Assignments/Exams:").pack()
        self.link_vars = {}
        for item_id, display_text in self.link_options.items():
            var = tk.BooleanVar()
            if note and item_id in note.get("linked_items", []):
                var.set(True)
            tk.Checkbutton(self.win, text=display_text, variable=var).pack(anchor="w")
            self.link_vars[item_id] = var

        tk.Button(self.win, text="Save Note", command=self.save_note).pack(pady=5)

    def get_linkable_items(self):
        # Scan assignments and exams for the student
        import os, json
        items = {}
        ASSIGNMENTS_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
        EXAMS_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"
        student_id = self.notebook.student_id

        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(ASSIGNMENTS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    a = json.load(f)
                items[a["id"]] = f"Assignment: {a['subject']} ({a['id']})"

        for file in os.listdir(EXAMS_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(EXAMS_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    e = json.load(f)
                items[e["id"]] = f"Exam: {e['subject']} ({e['id']})"

        return items

    def save_note(self):
        title = self.title_entry.get().strip()
        content = self.text_area.get("1.0", "end").strip()
        linked_items = [item_id for item_id, var in self.link_vars.items() if var.get()]

        if not title:
            from tkinter import messagebox
            messagebox.showwarning("Save Note", "Title cannot be empty.")
            return

        note_data = {
            "title": title,
            "content": content,
            "last_modified": datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
            "student_id": self.notebook.student_id,
            "linked_items": linked_items
        }

        path = os.path.join("student/student_resources/notes", f"{self.notebook.student_id}_{title}.json")
        with open(path, "w") as f:
            json.dump(note_data, f, indent=4)

        self.notebook.refresh_notes()
        self.win.destroy()
```

class ExamWindow:
    # ... existing code ...
    def show_linked_notes(self):
        linked_notes = []
        import os, json
        NOTEBOOK_DIR = "student/student_resources/notes"
        for file in os.listdir(NOTEBOOK_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.exam['student_id']}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                with open(os.path.join(NOTEBOOK_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                    note = json.load(f)
                    if self.exam["id"] in note.get("linked_items", []):
                        linked_notes.append(note["title"])
        if linked_notes:

### **1. Note Usage Analytics Module - `note_analytics.py`**

```python
import os
import json

NOTEBOOK_DIR = "student/student_resources/notes"

def load_all_notes(student_id=None):
    notes = []
    for file in os.listdir(NOTEBOOK_DIR):
        if file.endswith(".json"):
            if student_id and not file.startswith(f"{student_id}_"):
                continue
            with open(os.path.join(NOTEBOOK_DIR, file), "r") as f:
                notes.append(json.load(f))
    return notes

def compute_note_usage(student_id=None):
    notes = load_all_notes(student_id)
    usage_summary = {}
    for note in notes:
        usage_count = len(note.get("linked_items", []))
        usage_summary[note["title"]] = {
            "student_id": note["student_id"],
            "usage_count": usage_count,
            "linked_items": note.get("linked_items", [])
        }
    return usage_summary

def compute_subject_usage(student_id=None, assignment_subjects=None):
    """
    Optional: Compute note usage per subject.
    assignment_subjects: dict mapping assignment/exam ID to subject
    """
    usage_summary = compute_note_usage(student_id)
    subject_usage = {}
    for note_title, data in usage_summary.items():
        for linked_id in data["linked_items"]:
            subj = assignment_subjects.get(linked_id, "Unknown")
            subject_usage[subj] = subject_usage.get(subj, 0) + 1
    return subject_usage
```

## **1. Procedural Assignment/Exam Generator - Core Concept**

**Goals:**

1. Generate **assignments/exams** automatically for each student.
2. Select **questions/topics directly from GED textbooks**.
3. Store as **JSON files** for integration with notifications, research notes, and analytics.
4. Support **grading flags** for teachers and BoE QA review.

---

## **2. Folder Structure**

```
student/student_resources/
├── assignments/
├── exams/
├── textbooks/
└── notes/
```

- Each assignment/exam is a **JSON file**:

```json
{
    "id": "student123_Math_ASSIGN_20260130120000",
    "student_id": "student123",
    "subject": "Math",
    "type": "assignment",
    "questions": [
        {
            "chapter": "Numbers & Operations",
            "question": "Simplify: 3/4 + 5/8",
            "answer": "11/8"
        },
        ...
    ],
    "submitted": false,
    "graded": false,
    "score": null
}
```

---

## **3. Python Generator Script**

```python
import os
import json
import random
from datetime import datetime

TEXTBOOK_DIR = "student/student_resources/textbooks"
ASSIGNMENT_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAM_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"

os.makedirs(ASSIGNMENT_DIR, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(EXAM_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def load_textbook(subject_file):
    path = os.path.join(TEXTBOOK_DIR, subject_file)
    chapters = {}
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, "r") as f:
            lines = f.read().split("\n")
        current_chapter = None
        content = []
        for line in lines:
            if line.startswith("Chapter"):
                if current_chapter:
                    chapters[current_chapter] = " ".join(content)
                current_chapter = line
                content = []
            else:
                content.append(line.strip())
        if current_chapter:
            chapters[current_chapter] = " ".join(content)
    return chapters

def generate_assignment(student_id, subject, type_="assignment", num_questions=5):
    # Map subject to textbook filename
    subject_map = {
        "Math": "GED_Math.txt",
        "LanguageArts": "GED_LanguageArts.txt",
        "Science": "GED_Science.txt",
        "SocialStudies": "GED_SocialStudies.txt"
    }
    textbook = load_textbook(subject_map[subject])
    questions = []

    chapters = list(textbook.keys())
    for _ in range(num_questions):
        chapter = random.choice(chapters)
        content = textbook[chapter]
        question = f"Reference Chapter: {chapter}. Summarize or solve problem related to: {content[:60]}..."
        answer = "Student response required."
        questions.append({"chapter": chapter, "question": question, "answer": answer})

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d%H%M%S")
    file_id = f"{student_id}_{subject}_{type_[:5].upper()}_{timestamp}"
    assignment_data = {
        "id": file_id,
        "student_id": student_id,
        "subject": subject,
        "type": type_,
        "questions": questions,
        "submitted": False,
        "graded": False,
        "score": None
    }

    file_path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENT_DIR if type_=="assignment" else EXAM_DIR, f"{file_id}.json")
    with open(file_path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(assignment_data, f, indent=4)

    return file_id

# Example: Generate assignments for a student
student_id = "student123"
for subj in ["Math", "LanguageArts", "Science", "SocialStudies"]:
    generate_assignment(student_id, subj, type_="assignment")
    generate_assignment(student_id, subj, type_="exam")

print("Procedural assignments and exams generated successfully!")
```

## **1. Auto-Grading Core Module - `grading_system.py`**

```python
import os
import json

ASSIGNMENT_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAM_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"

def grade_objective_questions(assignment):
    """
    Automatically grades objective questions if 'answer' is provided as key solution.
    Returns number of correct answers and total questions.
    """
    correct = 0
    total = len(assignment["questions"])
    
    for q in assignment["questions"]:
        # Only auto-grade if 'solution' key exists
        if "solution" in q:
            student_response = q.get("answer", "").strip()
            if student_response == q["solution"]:
                correct += 1
    return correct, total

def update_assignment_score(file_path, score, graded=True):
    with open(file_path, "r") as f:
        data = json.load(f)
    
    data["score"] = score
    data["graded"] = graded
    
    with open(file_path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=4)
```

## **2. Teacher Review Interface**

```python
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
import json
import os

ASSIGNMENT_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAM_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"

class TeacherReview:
    def __init__(self, subject=None):
        self.subject = subject
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Teacher Assignment/Exam Review")
        self.root.geometry("800x600")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.listbox = tk.Listbox(self.root)
        self.listbox.pack(fill="both", expand=True)

        self.review_button = tk.Button(self.root, text="Review Selected", command=self.review_selected)
        self.review_button.pack(pady=5)

        self.load_assignments()

    def load_assignments(self):
        self.assignments = []
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENT_DIR):
            if file.endswith(".json"):
                path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENT_DIR, file)
                with open(path, "r") as f:
                    data = json.load(f)
                    if self.subject and data["subject"] != self.subject:
                        continue
                    self.assignments.append((file, data))
                    self.listbox.insert(tk.END, f"{data['id']} - {data['student_id']} - {data['subject']}")

    def review_selected(self):
        selected = self.listbox.curselection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("Review", "Select an assignment/exam first.")
            return
        file_name, data = self.assignments[selected[0]]
        ReviewWindow(file_name, data)

class ReviewWindow:
    def __init__(self, file_name, data):
        self.file_name = file_name
        self.data = data
        self.path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENT_DIR, file_name)

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title(f"Review: {file_name}")
        self.win.geometry("800x600")

        self.text = tk.Text(self.win, height=25)
        self.text.pack(fill="both", expand=True)
        self.text.insert("1.0", self.format_assignment())

        tk.Button(self.win, text="Submit Score", command=self.submit_score).pack(pady=5)

    def format_assignment(self):
        output = ""
        for i, q in enumerate(self.data["questions"], 1):
            output += f"Q{i} [{q['chapter']}]: {q['question']}\n"
            output += f"Student Answer: {q.get('answer','')}\n"
            if "solution" in q:
                output += f"Solution: {q['solution']}\n"
            output += "-"*60 + "\n"
        return output

    def submit_score(self):
        score = tk.simpledialog.askfloat("Score", "Enter score (0-100):")
        if score is not None:
            self.data["score"] = score
            self.data["graded"] = True
            with open(self.path, "w") as f:
                json.dump(self.data, f, indent=4)
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Score {score} saved for {self.file_name}")
            self.win.destroy()
```

## **1. Desktop Interface Design**

## **2. Python Tkinter Implementation**

```python
import os
import json
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
from datetime import datetime

TEXTBOOK_DIR = "student/student_resources/textbooks"
ASSIGNMENT_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
EXAM_DIR = "student/student_resources/exams"
NOTE_DIR = "student/student_resources/notes"

class StudentDesktop:
    def __init__(self, student_id):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title(f"Academy OS - Student Desktop ({self.student_id})")
        self.root.geometry("1000x700")

        self.tab_control = ttk.Notebook(self.root)
        self.tab_control.pack(expand=1, fill="both")

        self.create_textbooks_tab()
        self.create_notes_tab()
        self.create_assignments_tab()
        self.create_exams_tab()
        self.create_notifications_tab()

        self.root.mainloop()

    # ---------------- Textbooks ----------------
    def create_textbooks_tab(self):
        self.textbooks_frame = ttk.Frame(self.tab_control)
        self.tab_control.add(self.textbooks_frame, text="Textbooks")

        self.textbook_list = tk.Listbox(self.textbooks_frame)
        self.textbook_list.pack(side="left", fill="y", padx=5, pady=5)
        for file in os.listdir(TEXTBOOK_DIR):
            if file.endswith(".txt"):
                self.textbook_list.insert(tk.END, file)

        self.open_button = tk.Button(self.textbooks_frame, text="Open Textbook", command=self.open_textbook)
        self.open_button.pack(side="top", padx=5, pady=5)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(self.textbooks_frame, wrap="word")
        self.text_display.pack(side="right", expand=True, fill="both", padx=5, pady=5)

    def open_textbook(self):
        selected = self.textbook_list.curselection()
        if selected:
            filename = self.textbook_list.get(selected[0])
            path = os.path.join(TEXTBOOK_DIR, filename)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                content = f.read()
            self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
            self.text_display.insert(tk.END, content)

    # ---------------- Research Notes ----------------
    def create_notes_tab(self):
        self.notes_frame = ttk.Frame(self.tab_control)
        self.tab_control.add(self.notes_frame, text="Research Notes")

        self.notes_list = tk.Listbox(self.notes_frame)
        self.notes_list.pack(side="left", fill="y", padx=5, pady=5)
        self.refresh_notes_list()

        self.open_note_btn = tk.Button(self.notes_frame, text="Open Note", command=self.open_note)
        self.open_note_btn.pack(pady=5)
        self.new_note_btn = tk.Button(self.notes_frame, text="New Note", command=self.new_note)
        self.new_note_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.note_display = tk.Text(self.notes_frame, wrap="word")
        self.note_display.pack(side="right", expand=True, fill="both", padx=5, pady=5)

    def refresh_notes_list(self):
        self.notes_list.delete(0, tk.END)
        for file in os.listdir(NOTE_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                self.notes_list.insert(tk.END, file)

    def open_note(self):
        selected = self.notes_list.curselection()
        if selected:
            filename = self.notes_list.get(selected[0])
            path = os.path.join(NOTE_DIR, filename)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            self.note_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
            self.note_display.insert(tk.END, f"Title: {data['title']}\n\n{data['content']}")

    def new_note(self):
        NoteEditor(self.student_id, self.refresh_notes_list)

    # ---------------- Assignments ----------------
    def create_assignments_tab(self):
        self.assignments_frame = ttk.Frame(self.tab_control)
        self.tab_control.add(self.assignments_frame, text="Assignments")

        self.assignment_list = tk.Listbox(self.assignments_frame)
        self.assignment_list.pack(side="left", fill="y", padx=5, pady=5)
        self.refresh_assignments_list()

        self.open_assignment_btn = tk.Button(self.assignments_frame, text="Open Assignment", command=self.open_assignment)
        self.open_assignment_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.assignment_display = tk.Text(self.assignments_frame, wrap="word")
        self.assignment_display.pack(side="right", expand=True, fill="both", padx=5, pady=5)

    def refresh_assignments_list(self):
        self.assignment_list.delete(0, tk.END)
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENT_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                self.assignment_list.insert(tk.END, file)

    def open_assignment(self):
        selected = self.assignment_list.curselection()
        if selected:
            filename = self.assignment_list.get(selected[0])
            path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENT_DIR, filename)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            display_text = f"Assignment: {data['subject']}\n\n"
            for i, q in enumerate(data["questions"], 1):
                display_text += f"Q{i} [{q['chapter']}]: {q['question']}\n"
                display_text += f"Your Answer: {q.get('answer','')}\n\n"
            self.assignment_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
            self.assignment_display.insert(tk.END, display_text)

    # ---------------- Exams ----------------
    def create_exams_tab(self):
        self.exams_frame = ttk.Frame(self.tab_control)
        self.tab_control.add(self.exams_frame, text="Exams")

        self.exam_list = tk.Listbox(self.exams_frame)
        self.exam_list.pack(side="left", fill="y", padx=5, pady=5)
        self.refresh_exams_list()

        self.open_exam_btn = tk.Button(self.exams_frame, text="Open Exam", command=self.open_exam)
        self.open_exam_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.exam_display = tk.Text(self.exams_frame, wrap="word")
        self.exam_display.pack(side="right", expand=True, fill="both", padx=5, pady=5)

    def refresh_exams_list(self):
        self.exam_list.delete(0, tk.END)
        for file in os.listdir(EXAM_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                self.exam_list.insert(tk.END, file)

    def open_exam(self):
        selected = self.exam_list.curselection()
        if selected:
            filename = self.exam_list.get(selected[0])
            path = os.path.join(EXAM_DIR, filename)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            display_text = f"Exam: {data['subject']}\n\n"
            for i, q in enumerate(data["questions"], 1):
                display_text += f"Q{i} [{q['chapter']}]: {q['question']}\n"
                display_text += f"Your Answer: {q.get('answer','')}\n\n"
            self.exam_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
            self.exam_display.insert(tk.END, display_text)

    # ---------------- Notifications / Analytics ----------------
    def create_notifications_tab(self):
        self.notifications_frame = ttk.Frame(self.tab_control)
        self.tab_control.add(self.notifications_frame, text="Notifications & Analytics")

        self.notifications_text = tk.Text(self.notifications_frame, wrap="word")
        self.notifications_text.pack(expand=True, fill="both", padx=5, pady=5)

        self.update_notifications()

    def update_notifications(self):
        self.notifications_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, "=== Notifications ===\n")
        # Example: Show all graded assignments
        for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENT_DIR):
            if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
                path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENT_DIR, file)
                with open(path, "r") as f:
                    data = json.load(f)
                if data.get("graded", False):
                    self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"{data['subject']} Assignment graded: {data['score']}\n")
        self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, "\n=== End of Notifications ===")
```

## **3. Research Note Editor**

```python
class NoteEditor:
    def __init__(self, student_id, refresh_callback):
        self.student_id = student_id
        self.refresh_callback = refresh_callback

        self.win = tk.Toplevel()
        self.win.title("New Research Note")
        self.win.geometry("600x400")

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Title:").pack()
        self.title_entry = tk.Entry(self.win, width=60)
        self.title_entry.pack()

        tk.Label(self.win, text="Content:").pack()
        self.text_area = tk.Text(self.win, height=20, width=80)
        self.text_area.pack()

        tk.Button(self.win, text="Save Note", command=self.save_note).pack(pady=5)

    def save_note(self):
        title = self.title_entry.get().strip()
        content = self.text_area.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not title or not content:
            messagebox.showwarning("Save Note", "Title and content cannot be empty.")
            return
        note_data = {
            "title": title,
            "content": content,
            "last_modified": datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
            "student_id": self.student_id,
            "linked_items": []
        }
        path = os.path.join(NOTE_DIR, f"{self.student_id}_{title}.json")
        with open(path, "w") as f:
            json.dump(note_data, f, indent=4)
        self.refresh_callback()
        self.win.destroy()
```

Do you want me to implement **adaptive study recommendations next**?
user
Yes.
ChatGPT
Perfect - let's implement **adaptive study recommendations** for students in the Academy OS. This system will **analyze student behavior**, including textbook usage, note-taking, and assignment/exam performance, and then provide **personalized learning paths and suggestions** to optimize study efficiency.  

---

## **1. Core Concept of Adaptive Study Recommendations**

**Data Sources:**

1. **Textbook Access** - which chapters a student reads and how often.  
2. **Research Notes** - topics students create notes on and link to assignments/exams.  
3. **Assignment/Exam Performance** - scores and areas of weakness.  
4. **Teacher/BoE Feedback** - flagged chapters or recommended exercises.  

**Outcome:**  
- Generate **prioritized study suggestions** for each student.  
- Recommend chapters, exercises, and notes for review.  
- Encourage **balanced study across all GED subjects**.  

---

## **2. Python Implementation**

```python
import os
import json
from collections import defaultdict

TEXTBOOK_DIR = "student/student_resources/textbooks"
ASSIGNMENT_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
NOTE_DIR = "student/student_resources/notes"
RECOMMENDATION_DIR = "student/student_resources/recommendations"

os.makedirs(RECOMMENDATION_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def adaptive_study_recommendations(student_id):
    # 1. Analyze assignment/exam performance
    performance = defaultdict(list)  # subject -> list of scores
    for folder in [ASSIGNMENT_DIR, "student/student_resources/exams"]:
        for file in os.listdir(folder):
            if file.startswith(student_id) and file.endswith(".json"):
                path = os.path.join(folder, file)
                with open(path, "r") as f:
                    data = json.load(f)
                if data.get("graded") and data.get("score") is not None:
                    performance[data["subject"]].append(data["score"])

    avg_scores = {}
    for subj, scores in performance.items():
        if scores:
            avg_scores[subj] = sum(scores)/len(scores)
        else:
            avg_scores[subj] = None  # No data yet

    # 2. Analyze notes to see focus areas
    note_topics = defaultdict(int)
    for file in os.listdir(NOTE_DIR):
        if file.startswith(student_id) and file.endswith(".json"):
            path = os.path.join(NOTE_DIR, file)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            for chap in data.get("linked_items", []):
                note_topics[chap] += 1

    # 3. Generate recommendations
    recommendations = []
    for subj in ["Math", "LanguageArts", "Science", "SocialStudies"]:
        score = avg_scores.get(subj)
        if score is None or score < 70:
            recommendations.append(f"Review {subj} textbook chapters where your notes are sparse.")
        else:
            recommendations.append(f"Continue practicing {subj} to reinforce strengths.")

    # 4. Highlight specific chapters with low notes or low performance
    for file in os.listdir(TEXTBOOK_DIR):
        if file.startswith(f"GED_{subj}"):
            path = os.path.join(TEXTBOOK_DIR, file)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                chapters = [line for line in f if line.startswith("Chapter")]
            for chap in chapters:
                if note_topics.get(chap, 0) == 0:
                    recommendations.append(f"Consider taking notes on {chap} to strengthen understanding.")

    # Save recommendations as JSON for desktop access
    rec_path = os.path.join(RECOMMENDATION_DIR, f"{student_id}_recommendations.json")
    with open(rec_path, "w") as f:
        json.dump({"student_id": student_id, "recommendations": recommendations}, f, indent=4)

    return recommendations

# Example usage
student_id = "student123"
recs = adaptive_study_recommendations(student_id)
print("Adaptive Study Recommendations Generated:")
for r in recs:
    print("- ", r)
```

---

## **3. Features of Adaptive Recommendations**

1. **Personalized Learning**
   - Focuses on **weak areas**, low-performing subjects, or chapters with minimal notes.  

2. **Dynamic Updates**
   - Recommendations are **updated every time a new assignment is graded** or a note is created.  

3. **Integration with Student Desktop**
   - Recommendations can appear in the **Notifications & Analytics tab**.  
   - Clickable links can take students **directly to chapters or exercises**.  

4. **Teacher & BoE Oversight**
   - Teachers can see **student recommendations** and intervene if necessary.  
   - BoE can **audit student learning paths** for QA purposes.  

---

```

- Review Math textbook chapters where your notes are sparse.
- Continue practicing LanguageArts to reinforce strengths.
- Review Science textbook chapters where your notes are sparse.
- Continue practicing SocialStudies to reinforce strengths.
- Consider taking notes on Chapter 1: Numbers & Operations to strengthen understanding.
- Consider taking notes on Chapter 3: Geometry to strengthen understanding.
```

## **1. Updating the Student Desktop - Notifications/Recommendations Tab**

We'll modify the **Notifications & Analytics tab** to include **clickable recommendation links** that open **textbook chapters** or **notes**.

```python
def create_notifications_tab(self):
    self.notifications_frame = ttk.Frame(self.tab_control)
    self.tab_control.add(self.notifications_frame, text="Notifications & Recommendations")

    self.notifications_text = tk.Text(self.notifications_frame, wrap="word")
    self.notifications_text.pack(expand=True, fill="both", padx=5, pady=5)
    self.notifications_text.tag_configure("link", foreground="blue", underline=True)
    self.notifications_text.tag_bind("link", "<Button-1>", self.open_link)

    self.update_notifications()

def update_notifications(self):
    self.notifications_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
    self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, "=== Notifications ===\n\n")
    
    # Show graded assignments
    for file in os.listdir(ASSIGNMENT_DIR):
        if file.startswith(f"{self.student_id}_") and file.endswith(".json"):
            path = os.path.join(ASSIGNMENT_DIR, file)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            if data.get("graded", False):
                self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"{data['subject']} Assignment graded: {data['score']}\n")

    # Show adaptive study recommendations
    rec_path = os.path.join(RECOMMENDATION_DIR, f"{self.student_id}_recommendations.json")
    if os.path.exists(rec_path):
        with open(rec_path, "r") as f:
            rec_data = json.load(f)
        self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, "\n=== Adaptive Study Recommendations ===\n")
        for rec in rec_data["recommendations"]:
            start_index = self.notifications_text.index(tk.END)
            self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, rec + "\n")
            end_index = self.notifications_text.index(tk.END)
            # Add clickable link tag if reference a chapter or note
            if "Chapter" in rec:
                self.notifications_text.tag_add("link", start_index, end_index)
                self.notifications_text.tag_bind("link", "<Button-1>", self.open_textbook_link)
            elif "note" in rec.lower():
                self.notifications_text.tag_add("link", start_index, end_index)
                self.notifications_text.tag_bind("link", "<Button-1>", self.open_note_link)

    self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, "\n=== End of Notifications ===\n")

# ---------------- Link Handlers ----------------
def open_textbook_link(self, event):
    # Parse chapter name from clicked line
    line = self.notifications_text.get(f"{event.widget.index('current')} linestart", f"{event.widget.index('current')} lineend")
    for file in os.listdir(TEXTBOOK_DIR):
        if file.endswith(".txt"):
            path = os.path.join(TEXTBOOK_DIR, file)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                content = f.read()
            if line.split("Chapter")[1].strip().split(":")[0] in content:
                # Open in textbook display
                self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
                self.text_display.insert(tk.END, content)
                self.tab_control.select(self.textbooks_frame)
                break

def open_note_link(self, event):
    # Open note based on recommendation line
    line = self.notifications_text.get(f"{event.widget.index('current')} linestart", f"{event.widget.index('current')} lineend")
    for file in os.listdir(NOTE_DIR):
        if file.startswith(self.student_id) and file.endswith(".json"):
            path = os.path.join(NOTE_DIR, file)
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            if data["title"] in line:
                self.note_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
                self.note_display.insert("1.0", f"Title: {data['title']}\n\n{data['content']}")
                self.tab_control.select(self.notes_frame)
                break
```

3. **Clickable Notes**
   - If a recommendation mentions a **note**, clicking it opens the **research notes tab** to that note.  

4. **Dynamic Updates**
   - When **new assignments are graded or new notes are created**, recommendations and links automatically update.

## **1. Core Engagement Metrics**

## **2. Folder Structure for Analytics**

```
student/student_resources/analytics/
├── textbook_usage.json
├── notes_usage.json
├── assignment_usage.json
└── engagement_summary.json
```

Each file stores **timestamped logs** per student.

## **3. Python Tracking & Logging Module**

```python
import os
import json
from datetime import datetime

ANALYTICS_DIR = "student/student_resources/analytics"
os.makedirs(ANALYTICS_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def log_textbook_access(student_id, textbook_file, chapter, duration_sec):
    path = os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "textbook_usage.json")
    data = load_json(path)
    entry = {
        "student_id": student_id,
        "textbook": textbook_file,
        "chapter": chapter,
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        "duration_sec": duration_sec
    }
    data.append(entry)
    save_json(path, data)

def log_note_interaction(student_id, note_file, action):
    path = os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "notes_usage.json")
    data = load_json(path)
    entry = {
        "student_id": student_id,
        "note_file": note_file,
        "action": action,  # created/edited/viewed
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
    }
    data.append(entry)
    save_json(path, data)

def log_assignment_interaction(student_id, assignment_file, action, score=None):
    path = os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "assignment_usage.json")
    data = load_json(path)
    entry = {
        "student_id": student_id,
        "assignment_file": assignment_file,
        "action": action,  # opened/submitted/graded
        "score": score,
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
    }
    data.append(entry)
    save_json(path, data)

def load_json(path):
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, "r") as f:
            return json.load(f)
    return []

def save_json(path, data):
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=4)
```

---

## **4. Analytics Summary & Engagement Insights**

```python
def generate_engagement_summary(student_id):
    summary = {}
    
    # Textbook time spent
    textbook_data = load_json(os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "textbook_usage.json"))
    student_textbook = [e for e in textbook_data if e["student_id"] == student_id]
    summary["total_textbook_time_sec"] = sum(e["duration_sec"] for e in student_textbook)
    
    # Notes created
    notes_data = load_json(os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "notes_usage.json"))
    student_notes = [e for e in notes_data if e["student_id"] == student_id and e["action"]=="created"]
    summary["notes_created"] = len(student_notes)
    
    # Assignments completed
    assignments_data = load_json(os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "assignment_usage.json"))
    student_assignments = [e for e in assignments_data if e["student_id"] == student_id and e["action"]=="submitted"]
    summary["assignments_completed"] = len(student_assignments)
    
    # Average score
    graded = [e for e in assignments_data if e["student_id"] == student_id and e.get("score") is not None]
    if graded:
        summary["average_score"] = sum(e["score"] for e in graded)/len(graded)
    else:
        summary["average_score"] = None
    
    # Save summary
    path = os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "engagement_summary.json")
    all_summary = load_json(path)
    # remove old entry
    all_summary = [e for e in all_summary if e["student_id"] != student_id]
    all_summary.append({"student_id": student_id, "summary": summary, "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()})
    save_json(path, all_summary)
    
    return summary
```

- Feed **recommendations engine** for adaptive study paths:  
  - Low chapter reading → suggest reading.

  - Low scores → suggest review chapters or exercises.  

```python
# In the notifications tab update
summary = generate_engagement_summary(self.student_id)
self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"\n=== Engagement Summary ===\n")
self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"Total textbook time: {summary['total_textbook_time_sec']//60} minutes\n")
self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"Notes created: {summary['notes_created']}\n")
self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"Assignments completed: {summary['assignments_completed']}\n")
self.notifications_text.insert(tk.END, f"Average score: {summary['average_score']}\n")
```

## **1. Dashboard Features**

**Teacher/BoE Dashboard Capabilities:**

2. **Class/Cohort Analytics**
   - Compare students across **subjects, performance trends, and engagement patterns**.

4. **Recommendations Oversight**
   - Review **adaptive study recommendations** being issued.  
   - Adjust or approve guidance if necessary.

## **2. Python Tkinter Implementation**

```python
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk, messagebox
import os
import json

ANALYTICS_DIR = "student/student_resources/analytics"
ASSIGNMENT_DIR = "student/student_resources/assignments"
STUDENT_LIST = ["student123", "student456", "student789"]  # Example student IDs

class BoEDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Academy OS - BoE/Teacher Dashboard")
        self.root.geometry("1100x700")
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(self.root, columns=("Avg Score", "Textbook Time (min)", 
                                                     "Notes Created", "Assignments Completed"), show="headings")
        self.tree.heading("Avg Score", text="Avg Score")
        self.tree.heading("Textbook Time (min)", text="Textbook Time (min)")
        self.tree.heading("Notes Created", text="Notes Created")
        self.tree.heading("Assignments Completed", text="Assignments Completed")
        self.tree.pack(expand=True, fill="both")

        self.refresh_btn = tk.Button(self.root, text="Refresh Data", command=self.refresh_dashboard)
        self.refresh_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.flag_btn = tk.Button(self.root, text="Flag Selected Student", command=self.flag_student)
        self.flag_btn.pack(pady=5)

        self.refresh_dashboard()

    def refresh_dashboard(self):
        self.tree.delete(*self.tree.get_children())
        for student_id in STUDENT_LIST:
            summary = self.load_engagement_summary(student_id)
            avg_score = summary.get("average_score", 0)
            textbook_time = summary.get("total_textbook_time_sec",0)//60
            notes_created = summary.get("notes_created",0)
            assignments_completed = summary.get("assignments_completed",0)
            self.tree.insert("", tk.END, iid=student_id, values=(avg_score, textbook_time, notes_created, assignments_completed))

    def load_engagement_summary(self, student_id):
        path = os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, "engagement_summary.json")
        if os.path.exists(path):
            with open(path, "r") as f:
                all_summaries = json.load(f)
            for entry in all_summaries:
                if entry["student_id"] == student_id:
                    return entry["summary"]
        return {}

    def flag_student(self):
        selected = self.tree.selection()
        if not selected:
            messagebox.showwarning("Flag Student", "Select a student first.")
            return
        student_id = selected[0]
        # Create a QA flag file for teacher/BoE review
        flag_path = os.path.join(ANALYTICS_DIR, f"{student_id}_flagged.json")
        with open(flag_path, "w") as f:
            json.dump({"student_id": student_id, "flagged": True, "timestamp": str(datetime.now())}, f, indent=4)
        messagebox.showinfo("Flagged", f"Student {student_id} has been flagged for QA review.")
```

Outcome Projection Tables\n\nOutcome tables determine *how* results manifest.\n\n### 3.1 Outcome Schema\n\n```\nOutcomeProfile {\n  id\n  physicalEffectWeight\n  accessEffectWeight\n  perceptionEffectWeight\n  narrativeEffectWeight\n  mythicEffectWeight\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Example: Denied Access (Soft)\n\n```\nOutcomeProfile: DENIAL_SOFT\n\nphysicalEffectWeight: 0.1\naccessEffectWeight: 0.4\nperceptionEffectWeight: 0.7\nnarrativeEffectWeight: 0.6\nmythicEffectWeight: 0.0\n```\n\nMost denial is psychological.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Loader Responsibilities\n\n1. **File Parsing**\n   - Accepts JSON, YAML, or similar structured formats.\n   - Parses all tables into memory objects.\n\n2. **Reference Linking**\n   - Connects ObjectArchetypes to BiasProfiles, AuthorityRules, OutcomeProfiles.\n   - Ensures CorridorMutationRules reference valid triggers.\n\n3. **Default Fallbacks**\n   - Provides system defaults if a table is missing or incomplete.\n   - Logs warnings for missing optional entries.\n\n4. **Versioning**\n   - Checks table schema version compatibility.\n   - Handles table migrations if format changes.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Validator Responsibilities\n\n1. **Integrity Checks**\n   - Each ObjectArchetype must reference valid BiasProfile, AuthorityRules, OutcomeProfile.\n   - All IDs must be unique.\n   - All trigger references must resolve.\n\n2. **Authority Coherence**\n   - No authority loops (e.g., Faction depends on Object which depends on Faction without escape).\n   - Priorities are monotonic (lower number = higher authority).\n\n3. **Bias Sanity**\n   - BaseSuspicion between 0-1.\n   - FearAmplifier positive.\n   - ReinterpretIntent is valid enum.\n\n4. **Outcome Weight Sanity**\n   - All weights between 0.0 and 1.0.\n   - Sum of weights may exceed 1.0, but must not be negative.\n\n5. **Trigger Consistency**\n   - MythicFlag triggers reference valid world or object state variables.\n   - CorridorMutation triggers reference valid faction or misread thresholds.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Loader Algorithm (Pseudocode)\n\n```\nfunction LoadTables(directoryPath):\n  for each file in directoryPath:\n    parse file into tableObjects\n    if schemaVersion mismatch:\n        migrateTable(tableObjects)\n    linkReferences(tableObjects)\n  validateTables(tableObjects)\n  return tableObjects\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Validator Algorithm (Pseudocode)\n\n```\nfunction validateTables(tableObjects):\n  for each ObjectArchetype in tableObjects:\n    assert ObjectArchetype.biasProfile exists\n    assert ObjectArchetype.authorityRules exists\n    assert ObjectArchetype.outcomeProfile exists\n  \n  for each AuthorityRule in tableObjects:\n    assert priority >= 0\n    assert authorityHolder in [Object, Faction, Mythic, World]\n  \n  for each BiasRule in tableObjects:\n    assert 0 <= baseSuspicion <= 1\n    assert fearAmplifier > 0\n    assert reinterpretIntent in IntentEnum\n  \n  for each OutcomeProfile in tableObjects:\n    assert 0 <= all weights <= 1\n  \n  checkNoAuthorityLoops(tableObjects)\n  checkTriggerReferences(tableObjects)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Error Handling & Logging\n\n- Loader logs: parsing errors, missing tables, version mismatches\n- Validator logs: invalid references, impossible authority, weight violations\n- Critical errors halt loading; warnings continue with defaults\n\n---\n\n## 6. Extension Points\n\n- Table hot-reloading for live design testing\n- Schema validation via JSON/YAML schema definitions\n- Optional debug mode: prints full link graph\n\n---\n\n## 7. Implementation Notes\n\n- Loader returns **runtime-ready objects** for Object Interaction Resolver\n- Validator ensures **authoritative correctness** before simulation begins\n- ECS-compatible: tables produce components, archetypes, and state seeds\n\n---\n\n## 8. {"name":"The Academy - TypeScript Loader & Validator","type":"code/javascript","content":"// The Academy - Loader & Validator in TypeScript\n// Consumes: BiasProfiles, AuthorityRules, OutcomeProfiles, ObjectArchetypes, CorridorMutationRules, MythicFlags\n\nimport fs from 'fs';\nimport path from 'path';\n\n// -----------------------------\n// Types\n// -----------------------------\n\ntype IntentEnum = 'Observe' | 'Request' | 'Force' | 'Perform' | 'Desecrate' | 'Protect';\n\ntype BiasRule = {\n  condition: string;\n  reinterpretIntent: IntentEnum;\n  suspicionDelta: number;\n};\n\ntype BiasProfile = {\n  id: string;\n  baseSuspicion: number;\n  fearAmplifier: number;\n  rules: BiasRule[];\n};\n\ntype AuthorityRule = {\n  priority: number;\n  condition: string;\n  authorityHolder: 'Object' | 'Faction' | 'Mythic' | 'World';\n};\n\ntype OutcomeProfile = {\n  id: string;\n  physicalEffectWeight: number;\n  accessEffectWeight: number;\n  perceptionEffectWeight: number;\n  narrativeEffectWeight: number;\n  mythicEffectWeight: number;\n};\n\ntype ObjectArchetype = {\n  id: string;\n  defaultBiasProfile: string;\n  defaultAuthorityRules: string;\n  defaultOutcomeProfile: string;\n};\n\ntype CorridorMutationRule = {\n  trigger: string;\n  visualShift: string;\n  audioShift: string;\n  accessShift: string;\n};\n\ntype MythicFlag = {\n  id: string;\n  triggerCondition: string;\n  globalEffect: string;\n};\n\n// -----------------------------\n// Loader\n// -----------------------------\n\nexport class AcademyLoader {\n  tables: Record<string, any> = {};\n\n  constructor(private directory: string) {}\n\n  loadTables() {\n    const files = fs.readdirSync(this.directory);\n\n    for (const file of files) {\n      if (file.endsWith('.json')) {\n        const fullPath = path.join(this.directory, file);\n        const data = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf8'));\n        this.tables[path.basename(file, '.json')] = data;\n      }\n    }\n\n    this.linkReferences();\n    this.validateTables();\n\n    return this.tables;\n  }\n\n  // -----------------------------\n  // Reference Linking\n  // -----------------------------\n  private linkReferences() {\n    const archetypes: ObjectArchetype[] = this.tables['ObjectArchetypes'] || [];\n    const biasProfiles: BiasProfile[] = this.tables['BiasProfiles'] || [];\n    const authorityRules: AuthorityRule[] = this.tables['AuthorityRules'] || [];\n    const outcomeProfiles: OutcomeProfile[] = this.tables['OutcomeProfiles'] || [];\n\n    archetypes.forEach((obj) => {\n      if (!biasProfiles.find(b => b.id === obj.defaultBiasProfile)) {\n        console.warn(`Archetype ${obj.id} references missing BiasProfile ${obj.defaultBiasProfile}`);\n      }\n      if (!authorityRules.find(a => a.priority.toString() === obj.defaultAuthorityRules)) {\n        console.warn(`Archetype ${obj.id} references missing AuthorityRule ${obj.defaultAuthorityRules}`);\n      }\n      if (!outcomeProfiles.find(o => o.id === obj.defaultOutcomeProfile)) {\n        console.warn(`Archetype ${obj.id} references missing OutcomeProfile ${obj.defaultOutcomeProfile}`);\n      }\n    });\n  }\n\n  // -----------------------------\n  // Validator\n  // -----------------------------\n  private validateTables() {\n    const biasProfiles: BiasProfile[] = this.tables['BiasProfiles'] || [];\n    biasProfiles.forEach(b => {\n      if (b.baseSuspicion < 0 || b.baseSuspicion > 1) {\n        throw new Error(`BiasProfile ${b.id} baseSuspicion out of range`);\n      }\n      if (b.fearAmplifier <= 0) {\n        throw new Error(`BiasProfile ${b.id} fearAmplifier must be positive`);\n      }\n      b.rules.forEach(rule => {\n        if (!['Observe','Request','Force','Perform','Desecrate','Protect'].includes(rule.reinterpretIntent)) {\n          throw new Error(`BiasRule in ${b.id} has invalid reinterpretIntent`);\n        }\n      });\n    });\n\n    const outcomeProfiles: OutcomeProfile[] = this.tables['OutcomeProfiles'] || [];\n    outcomeProfiles.forEach(o => {\n      const weights = [o.physicalEffectWeight, o.accessEffectWeight, o.perceptionEffectWeight, o.narrativeEffectWeight, o.mythicEffectWeight];\n      weights.forEach(w => {\n        if (w < 0 || w > 1) throw new Error(`OutcomeProfile ${o.id} weight out of range`);\n      });\n    });\n\n    // Authority coherence check\n    const authorityRules: AuthorityRule[] = this.tables['AuthorityRules'] || [];\n    const holders = ['Object','Faction','Mythic','World'];\n    authorityRules.forEach(a => {\n      if (!holders.includes(a.authorityHolder)) {\n        throw new Error(`AuthorityRule ${JSON.stringify(a)} has invalid authorityHolder`);\n      }\n      if (a.priority < 0) throw new Error(`AuthorityRule ${JSON.stringify(a)} has negative priority`);\n    });\n\n    console.log('Validation complete.');\n  }\n}"}

```ts
interface EnvironmentState {
  lighting: number; // 0-1
  temperature: number; // degrees
  gravity: number; // multiplier
  hazards: string[]; // list of active hazards
}
```

interface PlayerSignal {

});\n  Object.keys(player.visibleStats).forEach(key => { expr = expr.replace(new RegExp(`\\b${key}\\b`, 'g'), player.visibleStats[key].toString()); });\n  Object.keys(world.factionTension).forEach(key => { expr = expr.replace(new RegExp(`\\b${key}\\b`, 'g'), world.factionTension[key].toString()); });\n  expr = expr.replace(/true/g, 'true').replace(/false/g, 'false');\n  try { return eval(expr); } catch { return false; }\n}\n\nfunction evaluateAlignment(player: PlayerSignal, object: any): boolean {\n  // Example spiritual / divine geometry check\n  const alignmentScore = (player.resonanceProfile.Presence || 0) + (player.resonanceProfile.Logic || 0);\n  return alignmentScore >= (object.requiredAlignment || 1);\n}\n\nfunction resolveInteraction(player: PlayerSignal, object: any, tables: any, world: WorldMemory): Outcome {\n  if (object.requiredPerk && !player.perks.includes(object.requiredPerk)) {\n    return { physicalChange: 0, accessShift: 0, perceptionFeedback: 0, narrativeMemory: 0, mythicRipple: 0 }; // cannot interact\n  }\n\n  const biasProfile = tables['BiasProfiles'].find((b: any) => b.id === object.defaultBiasProfile);\n  const outcomeProfile = tables['OutcomeProfiles'].find((o: any) => o.id === object.defaultOutcomeProfile);\n  const authorityRules = tables['AuthorityRules'];\n  const corridorRules = tables['CorridorMutationRules'];\n  const mythicFlags = tables['MythicFlags'];\n\n  let perceivedIntent: IntentEnum = player.intent;\n  biasProfile.rules.forEach((rule: any) => { if (evaluateCondition(rule.condition, player, world)) perceivedIntent = rule.reinterpretIntent; });\n\n  const applicableAuthorities = authorityRules.filter((a: any) => evaluateCondition(a.condition, player, world));\n  applicableAuthorities.sort((a: any, b: any) => a.priority - b.priority);\n  const resolvedAuthority = applicableAuthorities[0]?.authorityHolder || 'Object';\n\n  const outcome: Outcome = {\n    physicalChange: outcomeProfile.physicalEffectWeight,\n    accessShift: outcomeProfile.accessEffectWeight,\n    perceptionFeedback: outcomeProfile.perceptionEffectWeight,\n    narrativeMemory: outcomeProfile.narrativeEffectWeight,\n    mythicRipple: outcomeProfile.mythicEffectWeight\n  };\n\n  // Apply cooperative/divine effects\n  if (object.isDivine && player.perks.includes('Geomancer') && evaluateAlignment(player, object)) {\n    outcome.mythicRipple += 0.5;\n    world.activeMythicFlags['DivineGate'] = true;\n  }\n\n  if (resolvedAuthority === 'Mythic') outcome.mythicRipple += 0.2;\n  if (resolvedAuthority === 'Faction') outcome.accessShift += 0.1;\n\n  // Environmental impact example\n  outcome.envEffect = { lighting: (object.lightingImpact || 0) * (player.resonanceProfile.Presence || 1) };\n  world.environment.lighting += outcome.envEffect.lighting || 0;\n\n  if (player.intent !== perceivedIntent) world.misreads += 1;\n  if (world.misreads >= 3) {\n    world.factionTension['FactionA'] = (world.factionTension['FactionA'] || 0) + 0.1;\n    world.corridorScars.push(`Door misread at ${object.id}`);\n  }\n\n  corridorRules.forEach((rule: any) => { if (evaluateCondition(rule.trigger, player, world)) world.corridorState[object.id] = { visualShift: rule.visualShift, audioShift: rule.audioShift, accessShift: rule.accessShift }; });\n\n  mythicFlags.forEach((flag: any) => { if (evaluateCondition(flag.triggerCondition, player, world)) world.activeMythicFlags[flag.id] = true; });\n\n  return outcome;\n}\n\nfunction resolveConcurrentInteractions(players: PlayerSignal[], objects: any[], tables: any, world: WorldMemory) {\n  objects.forEach(obj => {\n    const intentGroups: Record<IntentEnum, PlayerSignal[]> = {};\n    players.forEach(p => { intentGroups[p.intent] = intentGroups[p.intent] || []; intentGroups[p.intent].push(p); });\n\n    Object.keys(intentGroups).forEach(intent => {\n      const group = intentGroups[intent as IntentEnum];\n      group.forEach(player => {\n        const outcome = resolveInteraction(player, obj, tables, world);\n        if (group.length > 1) {\n          outcome.physicalChange *= 1.1; // cooperative amplification\n          outcome.accessShift *= 1.1;\n        }\n      });\n    });\n  });\n}\n\n// -----------------------------\n// Initialize World & Tables\n// -----------------------------\n\nconst world: WorldMemory = {\n  misreads: 0,\n  factionTension: {},\n  corridorScars: [],\n  corridorState: {},\n  activeMythicFlags: {},\n  environment: { lighting: 1, temperature: 20, gravity: 1, hazards: [] }\n};\nconst tableDirectory = path.join(__dirname, 'sample_tables');\nconst loader = new AcademyLoader(tableDirectory);\nconst tables = loader.loadTables();\nconst objects = tables['ObjectArchetypes'];\n\nconst players: PlayerSignal[] = [\n  { id: 'Player1', intent: 'Request', resonanceProfile: { Presence: 0.8, Logic: 0.6 }, reputationVector: { FactionA: 0.5 }, visibleStats: { Strength: 0.3 }, recentHistory: [], perks: ['Geomancer'] },\n  { id: 'Player2', intent: 'Request', resonanceProfile: { Presence: 0.5, Logic: 0.9 }, reputationVector: { FactionA: 0.2 }, visibleStats: { Strength: 0.2 }, recentHistory: [], perks: [] },\n  { id: 'Player3', intent: 'Force', resonanceProfile: { Presence: 0.9, Logic: 0.4 }, reputationVector: { FactionB: 0.6 }, visibleStats: { Strength: 0.7 }, recentHistory: [], perks: [] }\n];\n\nresolveConcurrentInteractions(players, objects, tables, world);\nconsole.log('Final World State with Environment, Perks & Divine Effects:', world);"}]}
